President Yang Peng of the Third Branch of the High Court Gives a Lecture on the Current Situation and Prospects of China's Judiciary, Concluding with the Abolition of Extraterritoriality as the Goal and Contributing Greatly to the Improvement of China's Judicial System 110

According to the Shen Shi News Agency, Yang Peng, the current president of the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, is a veteran of the legal profession, and his scholarship and morality are admired by all. He was recently appointed by the Ministry of Justice and took office last month. At the invitation of the Soochow University Law School on Kunshan Road in this city at 6 p.m. on the 6th of this month, and with the attendance of more than 300 guests, professors, and students, President Wu Jingxiong presided over the event. After introducing President Yang, President Yang stood up and gave a lecture on "The Current Situation and Prospects of China's Judiciary." He first pointed out that the four characters "phenomenal harmony" are the standard for judging the quality of the judicial system. Then, he outlined the shortcomings of the current state of China's judiciary and the steps and methods for improvement. He concluded by emphasizing the goal of developing and expanding the inherent spirit of the rule of law in our country, improving the judicial system to adapt to the current social and economic situation, and abolishing the deformed consular jurisdiction. Combining facts and theories, his discussion was incisive and insightful, contributing greatly to the improvement of China's judicial system. The Shen Shi News Agency reporter specially obtained the original manuscript of his lecture, which is published below:

Everything in the universe takes phenomenal harmony as the ultimate in beauty and perfection. All administrative or judicial systems of a country are naturally no exception. In terms of justice, the past judicial situation in our country, viewed from a modern perspective, cannot completely satisfy or praise us. However, judging from the economic and social conditions of each era, it still does not lose its phenomenon of harmony. Those who have studied the history of our country's legal system can understand its outline. Since the Reform Movement of the late Qing Dynasty, all the old judicial systems and laws have gradually been changed, and the speed of change is like lightning. For example, in the early Republic of China, the trial system adopted a genuine four-level, three-instance system. Then, the primary trial was abolished, and a simple court was attached to the local trial court. Now, a three-level, three-instance system is adopted. In terms of law, most of the public law part, such as the criminal law and civil and criminal procedure laws, are changed every few years. Almost all the latest legal systems in the world are quickly adopted. Because of the speed of progress, facts and the environment cannot keep pace, and various phenomena of disharmony arise. For example, on the one hand, the judicial organ has new-style courts, and all organizations and trials are based on law. On the other hand, the county magistrate concurrently handles judicial affairs, and most county magistrates who are not familiar with the law bear the brunt of the trial responsibility, resulting in many illegal judgments. There are many such examples. Now, the following points are briefly described: 1. Improvement of the county magistrate's concurrent judicial duties; 2. Striving for completeness of current laws; 3. Full planning of talent and funds; 4. The connection between judicial organs and other organs.

The improvement of the county magistrate's concurrent judicial duties: At present, the county magistrates in various provinces who concurrently handle judicial affairs often do not try civil and criminal cases according to law. In criminal cases, some judges do not make judgments based on legal provisions but according to their own opinions. Some judges even exceed the requests of the parties and make judgments. There are countless illegal facts. Even if a small number of cases are judged correctly, they are often flawed when strictly applied. Since the initial foundation of the first instance is wrong, it is difficult to remedy the second instance. This is because the opportunity has passed (such as the death of witnesses, the destruction of physical evidence), and it is not easy to find the truth in the second instance. Therefore, the disadvantages of the county magistrate's concurrent judicial duties are undeniable. At present, the people of more than a thousand counties in our country are under this bad system. In other words, more than 300 million people across the country have not been protected by new-style courts. If this kind of county magistrate's concurrent judicial system is not improved, the current high-level courts are like buildings built on sandy ground, which will eventually collapse sooner or later. According to Article 9 of the current Court Organization Law, county or city shall establish a local court. However, if the area is small, several counties may establish a local court. If the area is vast, a branch of the local court may be established. From the perspective of the law itself, it is complete and flawless, with the ultimate in beauty and harmony. However, from the perspective of the central and local financial resources and judicial talents, it is difficult to complete and improve this comprehensive and complete judicial system in one fell swoop. Therefore, the legislative and judicial authorities can only seek remedial measures. The central government has decided to improve the county magistrate's concurrent judicial duties before local courts or branch courts are generally established in various counties, that is, to establish a county judicial office in counties where no courts have been established. The Provisional Regulations on the Organization of County Judicial Offices have been passed by the Legislative Yuan and submitted to the National Government for promulgation. The important points are: 1. The county judicial office has independent administrative powers of adjudication; 2. The judges are appointed by the president of the High Court and approved by the Ministry; 3. The prosecutorial duties are concurrently handled by the county magistrate. The important purpose of this system is to gradually eliminate the entrenched practice of not separating administration and justice, so as to cultivate the foundation for the establishment of local courts in various counties in the future. The completion of our country's judicial system, if the whole country from top to bottom holds on to perseverance and moves forward bravely, it is not difficult to achieve success in a timely manner. 4. Striving for completeness of current laws: Since the establishment of the National Government, various important laws in our country have been gradually formulated and promulgated. However, a few laws are actually very important and have close links with current laws, but they are still lacking. For example, the Compulsory Enforcement Law, the Non-Contentious Case Law, and the Deposit Law are all examples. Regarding the Compulsory Enforcement Law, the Ministry of Judicial Administration has drafted a draft for the Legislative Yuan's reference. The Legislative Yuan is currently deliberating. As for the Non-Contentious Case Law, the Deposit Law, and even the regulations on compensation for wrongful imprisonment, some people proposed them at the Judicial Conference last year, requesting their formulation. The conference has already discussed solutions. In the future, the Legal Research Association of the Judicial Yuan may discuss this and contribute opinions to legislation. The importance of the Compulsory Law, Non-Contentious Case Law, and Deposit Law has been explained in detail by legal scholars and does not need to be repeated. As for the regulations on compensation for wrongful imprisonment, that is, the so-called Criminal Damage Compensation Law, how important is it? It is necessary to say a few words briefly. The criminal damage compensation system originated in Europe. Its basic theory is that when a person harms another, he should restore the damage caused by his harmful behavior to its original state. The same is true between people in society and between the people and the organs. Why not the organs for the people? Because of this, criminal law scholar Helic strongly advocated the criminal compensation system in his book "Opinions on Important Points of French Criminal Legislation" in 1821. Scholars from various countries followed suit. Therefore, many European countries have enacted criminal damage laws, but there are slight differences in their names and methods of regulation. This regulation is extremely important, needless to say. However, how to formulate it and how to implement it need to be studied. It should be specifically stated in the appendix that all current laws and regulations related to agricultural and industrial relations, as well as administrative laws and regulations related to the economy, such as transportation, health, fishery, mining, and forestry, are of great importance to the national economy and the people's livelihood, as are other ordinary civil and criminal laws. On New Year's Day this year, President Chiang, who is also the President of the Executive Yuan, gave a speech with the theme of economic construction movement, elaborating on his grand vision for economic construction, with clear and detailed explanations. After listening to it, we believe that in order to achieve the perfect realization of the economic construction movement, the above-mentioned laws and regulations should not only strive for perfection, but also make the effectiveness of each law and regulation fully exerted, so as not to become empty clauses. Only then can the economic construction movement succeed. Originally, law and economy support each other and use each other. Talking about law without economy is only a shell. Talking about economy without law, the economy loses its physique. As evidenced by the economically developed countries today, there is no complete law to be the core, and then economic construction can be maintained. Do you doubt my words? Please close your eyes and think. The civil law and special civil law that you have learned, such as the Company Law, the Bill of Exchange Law, the Maritime Law, and the Insurance Law, are all benefactors who maintain or promote the economy. Without these laws, the modern economic system may still be in a backward era. 3. Full planning of talent and funds: The implementation of any system must have three essential elements: planning, talent, and funds. The three are interconnected and indispensable. With planning and funds but without talent, the matter cannot be done. With planning, talent, and funds, the matter cannot be done even more. Although the current judiciary in our country has detailed and excellent plans, it may inevitably face considerable difficulties in terms of talent and funds. In terms of talent, since the late Qing Dynasty, scholars studying law have sprung up at once. However, given the vast territory of our country, the large population, and the large number of affairs that the country should handle, this talent seems to be numerous on the surface, but in terms of proportions, it is actually insufficient for distribution. Judicial talent is extremely important for the quality of justice. With good laws but without good judges to apply them, good laws will also become bad laws. For example, the provisional attachment of the security procedures of civil litigation was originally a relief system specially set up by law to avoid the inability to enforce or the difficulty of enforcing in the future when the debtor fails to pay the money debt disputes. It is actually the best way to protect the interests of creditors in civil litigation. According to the provisions of the Civil Procedure Law, the applicant for provisional attachment does not have to provide security, and even if it is necessary to order it to provide security, it does not have to be limited to money. If the judge does not ask whether the applicant for provisional attachment is right or wrong, or whether its current economic situation is, it is generally ordered to provide a large amount of cash security, so that the parties regard the application for provisional attachment as a fear. Isn't a good law turned into a bad law? Conversely, if there are good judges, even if the law is bad, it will not cause harm. For example, the French Civil Code was formulated in the Napoleonic era. It is the oldest in the modern civil codes of various countries. There is a provision that when a wife engages in legal behavior, she should obtain the consent of her husband. However, the French court believes that the recent economic situation of individuals is contradictory. Therefore, there are precedents that recognize that a wife does not need to obtain the consent of her husband to enter into a labor contract with others. There are countless other similar examples. From this, it can be known that although the law is old, if excellent judges are used to apply it, it will not cause harm. Therefore, the rise and fall of judicial talent and the rise and fall of the judicial future are like shadows following the form. Now, in addition to expressing regret for the education authorities' policy of restricting legal education, we deeply admire the spirit of the central and provincial and municipal education authorities' efforts in legal education over the years. The Soochow University Law School has an excellent history and has produced many talents. This school occupies an important position in the cultivation of legal talents in our country at present and in the future, needless to say. As for the funding issue, the current situation in various provinces, except for the provinces with sufficient judicial funds, the salaries of judges in remote provinces are very meager, but their service spirit is not therefore slightly lazy. The virtuous morals of sages and sages who live in thatched cottages and eat with a bamboo basket and a gourd are deeply instilled in the hearts of the people. Therefore, even if the treatment is meager, it is not enough to discourage their ambitions. However, the responsibility of the judge lies in fairness and justice to administer judgments related to the life and property of the people. The importance of its position goes without saying. Most of the judges in the border areas of our country now understand the noble purpose of life, which is to seek bread for work, not to seek work for bread. However, if they are often given very meager treatment, it is not the way for the country to respect scholars and value justice. At last year's National Judicial Conference, it was decided that the judicial funds should be borne by the national treasury. At present, the central judicial authorities are working hard to realize this plan, so that the treatment of judges in various provinces will be equal and will not be thick or thin due to the wealth or poverty of local finances. The problem of judicial funding can also be resolved satisfactorily in the near future. 4. The connection between judicial organs and other organs: The composition of a country is like a machine. The various organs from the central to the local are no different from the gears or pistons in this machine. If one part of the machine is not working properly, it will affect the whole. If the effectiveness of one part of the national organs is hindered, it will affect other parts. The reason is very willing and does not need to be described in detail. Now, just take the point of judicial police as an example. According to Article 209 of the Criminal Procedure Law, police officers, military police officers, soldiers, and others who are authorized by law to exercise the powers of judicial police officers on specific matters are judicial police officers. Regarding the investigation of crimes, they shall listen to the command of the procurator. Article 210 of the same law stipulates that when the police, military police, and others who are authorized by law to exercise the powers of judicial police on specific matters exercise the powers of judicial police, they shall listen to the order of the procurator regarding the investigation of crimes. However, in reality, it is not the case. Therefore, the activities of the police power are seriously affected. The command or order of the judicial police to investigate crimes is actually the soul of the inspection system. The above-mentioned defects were seen by the Ministry of Judicial Administration early on. Each department related to the year will consult with each other on this issue to improve the evidence of the procurator's command and the related agencies will be printed and implemented. Since its implementation, it has been quite convenient. In addition, the Ministry of Judicial Administration has recently formulated a charter for the allocation of judicial police in accordance with the Court Organization Law. It is currently consulting with relevant departments. The mission of this charter is to seek to effectively establish contact between judicial organs and military and police and other administrative or transportation organs within the scope prescribed by laws and regulations, so as to achieve the goal of completely investigating crimes, so that the various provisions of the Criminal Procedure Law regarding the procurator's command and order of the judicial police will not be the same as being empty. The above points are all the current situation of judicial improvement in our country and its future prospects. From the current situation, there is only progress and no regression. No one can deny it. What is even more advanced is that our country is working hard on judicial improvement from top to bottom. Progress is the duty of the government and people of a country under the rule of law. At the same time, we also hope that the current consular jurisdiction that is being restricted can be lifted immediately. The existence of consular jurisdiction not only harms our country's sovereignty, but also hinders international commerce and causes legal conflicts. The people of countries that enjoy this right do not see its convenience. This aspiration of abolishment has been forgotten by people from all walks of life in our country, and insightful people from foreign countries also deeply expect it. In short, the country is now in a difficult situation. We are working hard for the rule of law internally and fighting for national rights externally. This sacred duty is actually the goal of all legal scholars. What has been said today is only a general outline for your study.

Fu'an Company Amusement Park Experiencing a False Alarm Due to a Fire in a Neighboring Business; Fire Tongue Sneaks into the Amusement Park from the Third Floor of a Ginseng Shop; Tourists Flee in Panic, Escalator Collapses, Several People Injured 122

The Fu'an Company Amusement Park at the corner of Dongmen Road in the Nanshi district experienced a chaotic scene last night around 6 p.m. During the initial performance of the four-part "Peng Gong'an," the park was swarming with visitors because it was a Saturday. The front gate of the park is under the jurisdiction of the Yiting Police Station, while the rear gate falls under the jurisdiction of the Shiliupu Sub-bureau. Unexpectedly, a fire broke out on the third floor of the Yongyutai Ginseng Shop next to the rear gate, immediately filling the air with thick smoke. Soon flames burst through the roof. The northern wind fanned the flames directly toward the third-floor windows of the amusement park. Tourists were horrified and began fleeing. Many ignorant women and children wailed and screamed, creating chaos. Those who tried to escape using the rear staircase were crushed and trampled in the rush. The iron supports on the lower level buckled, and the cement handrail collapsed, causing men and women tourists to fall from the stairs. Some were unable to get up immediately and were trampled and injured. A 17-year-old Ningbo native named Fang Xianming sustained the most serious injuries and lost consciousness. Fortunately, police officers stationed at the park made every effort to control the crowd. They rescued Fang and sent him to Nanyang Hospital for treatment. Doctors reported that his condition was critical. An elderly woman, a middle-aged woman, and a girl were also injured, and their families took them to the hospital for treatment. The incident was reported to the Yiting Police Station. Chief Yu personally led officers to investigate the scene and planned to report to the General Bureau for instructions.

Geng Zhaolin Uses Street Magic for Fraud; Elementary School Student Swindled Out of Gold Ring; Geng Zhaolin Sentenced to Four Months 124

Xiao Hongying, a 12-year-old Cantonese boy residing at No. 12, Tianshui Road, was walking home from school around 11:30 a.m. on July 24th of last year when he saw Geng Zhaolin, a native of Suzhou, setting up a stall near the intersection of North Henan Road and Tianshui Road to perform magic tricks. He had hung a white cloth with the words "Living Magic Research Society" written on it, advertising various acts such as "Immortal Picking Beans," "Fetching Water Across the Mountain," and "Flying Star Playing Cards." He held a deck of playing cards and threw them into the air as he performed his skills (i.e., Flying Star Playing Cards). The boy was delighted and asked to learn the tricks. Geng Zhaolin said that those who wished to learn this skill must give him a piece of gold jewelry for him to pray over, after which the magic would be particularly effective. Xiao went home and obtained a gold ring worth six yuan from his sister and handed it over to Geng. Geng folded a piece of white paper with the four characters "Flying Star Playing Cards" written on it and told the boy to quickly return home and open it to understand the trick, and then come back to ask him if he wanted to learn more. The boy ran home and opened the paper, only to find the same four characters written on it. When he went back to the spot, Geng had vanished. The boy realized he had been cheated and could only cry and tell his sister. The afternoon before yesterday, Xiao was passing by North Xizang Road when he saw Geng using the same method to trick other children into learning magic tricks. He immediately called Hua Pu at No. 300 and detective Chen Xikang, who arrived and arrested Geng. They took the white cloth sign for the "Living Magic Research Society" and a deck of playing cards to the Hongkou Police Station for custody. The day before yesterday, they were transferred to the Third Criminal Court of the First Court. Zhang Shizhu, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, briefly described the previous events and requested an investigation. The detective and Xiao described the events, and the evidence was presented for inspection. The defendant bowed his head without a word and begged for leniency. Judge Jiang Shuzi sentenced Geng Zhaolin to four months in prison, and the evidence was confiscated.

Collection Officer Commits Suicide Due to Inability to Repay Debts; Autopsy to be Performed by the Court Today 125

Tang Baixiang, a 24-year-old native of Suzhou residing at No. 47, Lane 2, New Zhazha Road, in the Public Concession, worked as a collection officer at the Dachang Automobile Manufacturing and Repair Factory at Nos. 59 and 60, Wusongjiang Road, in the French Concession. Recently, it was discovered by his employer that he had embezzled more than 40 yuan, and he was ordered to repay it by the 6th of this month. Although Tang agreed, he was unable to raise the funds, which led him to contemplate suicide. Using the alias Shi Junji, he went to the Anshang Inn at No. 35, West Xinzha Bridge Street, in the French Concession on the night of the 5th and booked Room No. 6. He got up and went out around 10:00 AM on the 6th, purchased raw opium, and returned to the inn around 1:00 PM, where he closed the door and lay down to smoke the opium and commit suicide. Around 5:30 PM in the evening, he groaned in pain from the poison. The tea server, Yao Bangrui, noticed and knocked on the door, but there was no response. The door was bolted from the inside, so he pried open the window and saw Tang lying in bed after taking poison, on the verge of death. He immediately informed the front desk and reported to the French Police Station, who summoned an ambulance and rushed to the scene. Tang was sent to Renji Hospital, but he was already too deeply poisoned and could not be saved. He died at 4:30 AM yesterday morning. The hospital notified the police, who transported the body to the autopsy room of the Tongren Fuyuan Branch, informed the family, and reported to the court for an examination today.

Two Dance Schools Prosecuted for Privately Selling Dance Tickets; Yao Changyu Fined Twelve Yuan; Xu Zhiyi's Part to be Heard Later 127

Yao Changyu, who runs the Da Shanghai Dance School at No. 592, opposite the YMCA on Sichuan Road in the Public Concession, and Xu Zhiyi, who runs the Far East Women's Travel Agency in Room 516 on the ninth floor of the Continental Department Store on Nanjing Road, were previously prosecuted by the police for selling dance tickets without obtaining a license from the Public Works Department, each fined eight yuan, and ordered to obtain the license. Yesterday morning, the court ordered Yao Changyu and Xu Zhiyi to appear in court for questioning. Xu failed to appear, and only Yao complied. Last night at 10:00 PM, he and Western Inspector Watson went to inform Yao that he was to appear in court today. They found many dancers at the school, and a woman was selling dance tickets at the counter. They immediately confiscated the dance tickets and ordered that they be retrieved after today's court hearing. Unexpectedly, Yao, after seeing them leave around 12:00 AM, falsely reported to the General Patrol Room that a Chinese detective and a Westerner had arrived and forcibly snatched the dance tickets. This was not true. After Judge Shen questioned Yao, he immediately sentenced Yao Changyu to a fine of twelve yuan. Xu Zhiyi's part was postponed for further review.

Shanghai Journalists Association Holds Spring General Meeting Yesterday; Due to Insufficient Quorum, Preliminary Resolution to Amend the Association's Constitution; Next General Meeting Will Elect With One-Quarter Attendance 128

The Shanghai Journalists Association held its fifth spring general meeting yesterday (the 7th) at 2:00 PM at the YMCA on Sichuan Road. Ninety-three members attended. Huang Xianggu, a representative from the Municipal Party Committee, Hong Kui, a representative from the Municipal Government, and Lei Kenan, a representative from the Social Affairs Bureau, all attended to provide guidance. Because the number of attendees did not meet the quorum, the meeting proceeded according to Article 31 of the Association's Constitution (if the number of attendees is less than half but occupies one-quarter of the total membership, the meeting can still be held, but all resolutions passed at the meeting can only be regarded as preliminary resolutions). The following is a record of the meeting:

Meeting Proceedings

After the usual formalities, in addition to Yan Duhe, Tang Shichang, and Hang Shijun, who were recommended by the Executive and Supervisory Committees as chairmen of the meeting, Qu ShaoYi and Zhao Junhao were also elected as chairmen on the spot. Chairman Yan Duhe led the attendees in performing the formalities and gave an opening speech. Then, Huang Xianggu, a representative from the Municipal Party Committee, gave a speech, encouraging everyone to unite and serve the Party and the country. Next, Lei Kenan, a representative from the Social Affairs Bureau, gave a speech, stating that the news media is the driving force behind social culture and education, and he hoped that everyone would work hard to promote it and fulfill their responsibility as the voice of the people. Immediately afterward, the discussion of the proposals began. The proposal to establish a sports meet for journalists to improve their health was rejected. The proposal to organize a national journalists association to strengthen unity was put on hold. The proposal to improve the association's affairs was decided to be handled by the Executive Committee. The proposal to amend the association's constitution and change the election method was approved in principle and referred to the next Executive Committee to formulate measures. All of the above resolutions were made as preliminary resolutions and will be subject to formal resolutions at a reconvened members' meeting.

Amending the Constitution

Subsequently, Qian Hua, Yan Esheng, Yuan Yeyu, Zhang Jiping, Qian Cangshuo, and others proposed amending the constitution to remedy the lack of a quorum. As a result of the discussion, Article 32 of the constitution was amended to read: "If the number of attendees at the election meeting is insufficient for a quorum, a new members' meeting shall be convened, and the election shall be conducted when one-quarter of the total membership is present." This preliminary resolution, after being passed by the next general meeting (with one-quarter of the members present), can be implemented.

Chinese Ancient Coin Society Authenticates the Manufacturing Location of the Anyang Knife Coin 129

The Chinese Ancient Coin Society held its fourth research meeting yesterday. The research topic was the "Anyang Knife." Regarding the Anyang Knife among the Qi knife coins, everyone knows about it, but the explanations recorded in *Ji Jin Suo Jian Lu* and *Gu Quan Hui Huo Bu Wen Zi Kao* are all mistaken. Even *Qian Lue,* *Pi Tan,* and *Yi Qie Lu* have failed to accurately point out the location of Anyang. The society has now authenticated the manufacturing location of the Anyang Knife, which is the Anyang mentioned in the *Annals of Xiang Yu* in the *Records of the Grand Historian*: "King Huai of Chu ordered Wang Yi to rescue Zhao, who traveled to Anyang and stayed there for forty-six days without advancing." The city of Anyang is located east of Cao County in Yanzhou Prefecture, as seen in the *Comprehensive Gazetteer*. Based on this, it can be proven that the various coin catalogues are mistaken and their omissions can be supplemented. Furthermore, the first issue of "Ancient Coin Studies," compiled by the society, has already been published. The cover was inscribed by Ye Gongchuo, the vice president of the society. The content includes Zheng Jiaxiang's "Evolution and Changes of Ancient Currency," Chen Rentao's "An Overview of the Evolution of Script Styles in Coin Inscriptions," Ding Fu Bao's "On the Shortcomings of Ancient Coin Collectors' Lack of Knowledge of Weights and Measures," Xu Jiqing's "Preface to Rubbings of Modern Coins," and Yang Kailing's "Biography of Mr. Bao Zinian." The unpublished manuscripts of Weng Yiquan, Rao Dengzhi, and others are particularly rare and valuable. Starting today, they are sold by the Medical Book Bureau on Meibaige Road and the Shanghai Magazine Company on Fourth Malu.

Jiangsu Farmers Bank Promotes Rural Cooperative Enterprises in the Suburbs of Shanghai 130

According to Shen Shi News Agency, the Shanghai Branch of the Jiangsu Farmers Bank, recognizing the importance of the rural economy in the suburbs of Shanghai, has jointly promoted cooperative enterprises with the Yutang Public Education Center, using Yutang as the center and gradually expanding. The cooperative societies approved by the bank for loans include the Yutang, Qingdeng, Lincun, and Maqiao cooperative societies. Cooperative loans are intended for productive enterprises. Loan methods, except for marketing operations, mostly adopt the method of lending physical goods. The bank guides the various cooperative societies in handling these matters. The total amount of loans issued last year was nearly 100,000 yuan, with excellent results. This year, two more central areas have been identified for active expansion. Because Shanghai County is divided into two major regions by the Huangpu River running through the center, making transportation quite inconvenient, the bank's management of cooperative enterprises throughout the county is also divided into eastern and western districts. The western districts are promoted by the bank's Beiqiao office, while the eastern districts are directly handled by the Shanghai Branch.

Recent Business Situation of Chinese and Foreign Match Companies 131

The various brands of matches produced by the Chinese match companies are sold in various ports and have been doing very well in business. Recently, due to the impact of smuggling, losses have resulted. The manufacturing cost of raw materials has increased, as well as labor costs, now requiring an increase of three to four yuan per case. It is said that starting on the 15th of this month, Chinese and foreign match companies will temporarily increase the price by three yuan per case to maintain capital. According to cigarette and money exchange businesses yesterday, the sales volume of matches has been the highest for the Phoenix brand. Later, it was said that the brand had a certain foreign shareholder and partnered with the Suisheng Company. After this news spread, business failed and plummeted. It was then sold to the Meiguang Company, which established a factory in Shanghai for manufacturing, with the certification of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, issuing sales, and hiring Mr. Chen Ronglu as the salesman. Mr. Chen and the leaders of the Chinese factories sought a consensus and organized a joint office and management committee to rectify market prices and maintain business tax revenue, benefiting both taxpayers and businesses. It has been three years since then, and the factories' businesses have gradually developed, with profits increasing significantly in recent years. Chinese matches account for 85% of the sales volume, while the Phoenix brand and other products of the Meiguang Company account for 15%.

National Goods Maintenance Association: Petition for Adoption of Domestically Produced Raincloth, and a Request to Increase Import Tariffs on Foreign Raincloth; Explanation of Three Points Distinguishing Domestic and Non-Domestic Goods 132

The China National Goods Maintenance Association, on the basis of a letter from the Lianpu Company explaining three points distinguishing domestic raincoats, oilcloth, and other goods from non-domestic goods, has forwarded a petition requesting that all government agencies be ordered to thoroughly investigate merchants and purchasing agents who obscurely pass off foreign goods as domestic, thereby hindering the progress of domestic goods. They also request that an order be issued to uniformly adopt the “Flying Eagle” brand of domestically produced goods, and to increase import tariffs on foreign raincloth and similar items to promote domestic industry. The Association recently submitted a document to the Executive Yuan, stating, "We are submitting this petition to earnestly request that all government agencies be notified to pay attention to the three points that distinguish domestically produced raincloth, oilcloth, waterproof cloth, and other goods from foreign products. They should uniformly adopt the “Flying Eagle” brand of domestically produced raincloth, oilcloth, and other products, and increase import tariffs on foreign raincloth and similar items, to promote domestic industry.

Regarding the matter of promoting domestic industry, the Association has recently received a letter from Liang Shixiong, manager of the Lianpu Trading Co., Ltd. Waterproof Cloth Factory, stating, in brief, 'Our factory was established with capital raised by Chinese citizens. The "Flying Eagle" brand of military oilcloth, raincloth, and various other domestic raincloth, raincoat silk, and waterproof cloth items are all meticulously researched and manufactured by our factory manager, who serves as the technician. Moreover, the raw materials and base cloth are all purchased domestically. Our products are reliable and our reputation is solid. We have consistently received registration and awards from the Ministry of Military Affairs, the Ministry of Industry, and the Ministry of Finance, and have been thoroughly inspected by national goods organizations, which have recognized us as a genuine domestic manufacturer. However, our factory is not complacent and strives for continuous improvement in our products, sparing no effort. As a result, the quality of our products improves daily, and production is accelerating. We hope that after sales promotion, foreign goods on the market will disappear and be unable to be sold. Our domestically produced goods, with the promotion from above and below, should be able to spread quickly and be widely sold on the market. Recently, a small number of unscrupulous merchants, seeking only their own small profits and disregarding the public good of the Chinese people, have falsely claimed that imported foreign raincloth and oilcloth are domestically produced, requesting various

Military and Government Agencies

to inspect and adopt them. This prevents our genuine domestic goods from being sold. Obstructing the business of our domestic factories is a minor matter; what about the outflow of rights and interests? Upon comparing domestic and foreign raincloth and oilcloth, the obvious key points are: the width and dimensions of the base cloth. Domestic cloth, such as that from Yong'an, Shenxin, and the Suzhou Weaving Factory, is only 35 to 38 inches wide at most, while foreign cloth is as wide as 42 to 44 inches. This wide-width base cloth, if one wants to pass it off as domestic, is not only unavailable in all of Shanghai, but also no domestic cloth factory in our entire country has such wide looms to weave it. This is the first point. The selvage of domestic base cloth is invariably stamped with the trademark of the weaving factory, while foreign cloth is not. This is the second point. The cotton yarn used for domestic base cloth is all purchased by the cloth factory after the resident unified tax office personnel have issued unified tax permits. After weaving, a woven product transport permit must be exchanged with the unified tax permit before it can be transported and sold. As for foreign goods, there are no such unified tax permits or transport permits. This is the third point. Therefore, we

request your Association

to truthfully forward this to the Executive Yuan

earnestly requesting a thorough investigation

of the fraudulent behavior of the aforementioned unscrupulous merchants, and to take measures to ban the practice of passing off foreign goods as domestic. On the one hand, please notify all relevant agencies to uniformly adopt our factory's "Flying Eagle" brand of domestically produced raincloth, oilcloth, and other items to promote domestic industry. Our factory would be most fortunate, and the domestic goods industry would be most fortunate. Enclosed are samples of our trademarked products and grey cloth, which we hope will also be forwarded to demonstrate our public-spiritedness.' The Association also received trademarked samples. Based on this, we

find that the company is currently the only domestic waterproof cloth factory, with the "Flying Eagle" brand, which was approved and registered by the Ministry of Industry and the Trademark Bureau in August of the 24th year of the Republic of China. Its products include military raincloth, oilcloth, raincoat silk, and waterproof cloth, etc. Its raw materials are white grey cloth woven by Chinese-owned yarn factories such as Yong'an, Shenxin, and the Suzhou Weaving Factory, meticulously processed and manufactured to be truly completely domestic goods. However, the width of its goods is only 38 inches at most, not as wide as foreign goods, which can be up to 44 inches. At this time, when tax-evading private smuggling is rampant in North China, private goods from both domestic and foreign locations are arriving like a tide. Our domestic manufacturers are alarmed, fearing destruction. We urgently hope that the government will

strictly combat smuggling

and set an example by earnestly purchasing domestic goods to maintain the industry. If purchasing agents in various government agencies are careless and allow unscrupulous merchants to deceive them with clever words, they will easily be misled, defeating the purpose of promoting domestic goods by your esteemed Yuan. For the sake of thoroughly investigating the truth, the Association, after a resolution by the fourth executive committee meeting, specially dispatched an investigator who secretly investigated and confirmed that the aforementioned wide-width raincloth and other goods are indeed foreign goods. The only domestic raincloth factory is Lianpu Trading Company. At this time when the government is earnestly promoting domestic goods, the Association, having learned this, should offer its opinion. Therefore, we are submitting this petition with the facts, and enclosing samples of domestic and foreign raincloth, oilcloth, raw material grey cloth, trademark styles, and photographs of registration certificates. We humbly beseech your esteemed Yuan to investigate and approve, instructing all government agencies to thoroughly investigate merchants who obscurely pass off foreign goods as domestic goods, hindering the progress of domestic goods, and requesting that an order be issued to uniformly adopt the "Flying Eagle" brand of domestic raincloth and oilcloth. At the same time, please instruct the Ministry of Finance to increase import tariffs on foreign raincloth and similar items, thereby promoting domestic goods and maintaining the livelihoods of industry and commerce. We await your order with utmost urgency, and respectfully request your instructions for compliance. Respectfully submitted, Chiang, President of the Executive Yuan.

Neighbors said that there had been no robbers. As for the rice in the shop, it was said that the shop's own trucks had been used to transport it to the countryside. It was then realized that it was a false report of robbery. The detectives returned to their bureaus and secretly dispatched detectives Yang Yucai and Xiao Huaiyu to lie in ambush near the shop to observe any movements inside. Yesterday (i.e., the 6th) afternoon, at around 4 PM, [Li Shusheng] told me to deliver a note to the back door of the Yong'an Company on Er Ma Road, and give it to shareholder Song Lansheng. I waited for about an hour but did not see Song Lansheng arrive. Moreover, when Li gave me the note, he also told me not to return to the shop at night, so I went to stay overnight at my aunt's house at the Wang Dachang Incense Shop nearby. This morning, I returned to the shop and saw that the situation inside was not right, and that fifty or sixty dan of white rice were missing. So I was observing from outside. Song Lansheng is about 30 years old this year, and is from Jiading. Li Shusheng is about 25 or 26 years old, and is from Dachang. I don't know where they are now. I didn't return to the shop last night, so I don't know about the police report, etc. After receiving the report, detectives Yang and Xiao took Li Jinxian into custody. They are now sending for Li Shusheng and Song Lansheng to be brought to the case for questioning.

Chinese detective Jin Wanrong from the Yulin Road Police Station apprehended Wang Fucheng, a native of Tongzhou, who was selling the drug "red pills" at Huasheng Road at about 10 PM the night before last. The police then secretly went to the address and arrested the assistant offender Wang Chujiu of Nanjing after being informed, as the principal offender Zhang Mazi had already fled. They took a total of Wang Ganxiang, Xi Xiaodi, Tang Gengen, and Wang Chujiu. They were also brought into the police station along with drug paraphernalia. One night ago, he was sent to the Second Criminal Chamber of the First Special Court. The judge, Jiang Shuzhi, interrogated each of the defendants and ordered their continued detention to await sentencing.

Hua Haiyang Company: Appeal for Return of Lace Samples 150

The Dutch merchant Hua Haiyang Company had previously ordered a large quantity of lace from the Xiehe Lace Company on Jingyuan Street, Guangdong Road. A dispute arose over payment for the goods. Zhu Dexin, from the lace company, hired attorney Yue Junying to accuse the foreign manager of the Hua Haiyang Company, the Austrian Mei Pisi, of colluding with Hua Jing, whom he had never met, to deduct the payment, and attempting to renege on the samples, etc., at the First Special District Local Court. The first instance judgment ordered the two defendants to jointly and severally repay the outstanding payment and return 191 pieces of hemp lace. However, the plaintiff's request for the return of 53 samples was rejected. They were unwilling to accept this and hired attorney Yue to file an appeal, stating that it is customary in the lace industry for goods to be received and delivered based on credit. Therefore, the samples held by the appellee were all marked and numbered so that foreign merchants could select them according to the numbers. After the payment was deducted, the appellee refused to return the samples, except for those that had already been retrieved. As these samples of Feili brand are of many colors and patterns, foreign orders depend entirely on the samples. Without the samples, the lace business would be suspended. At the time, in order to be accommodating, the company temporarily agreed to leave the samples in storage. It was not known that they intended to attempt to default. During the first trial, they even presented the appellant's receipt, claiming that they had been returned on January 7. However, the receipt clearly stated that the goods of Feili were returned, not that the samples were being returned. The original trial did not investigate thoroughly and rejected this part, which is difficult to accept. Moreover, after the return of the goods, repeated requests were made for the return of the samples, and the appellee's reply did not deny it, which is sufficient to prove that the samples had not actually been returned. Therefore, they requested a judgment ordering their return, and bearing the costs of litigation for both trials. The other day, the Civil Court of the Second Branch of the High Court summoned both parties and Zhang Tingrong and Zhang Lingsheng, who were present to witness the return of the goods, to appear in court for review. They ordered that the case be adjourned for further review.

To promote the use of domestically produced goods by Chinese working women and to provide guidance on the selection of materials and styles for summer clothing, a special international working women's fashion show was held at 5:30 PM the day before yesterday at the Shanghai YWCA at 999 Jing'an Temple Road. Recent News from Health World Monthly 152

Health World Monthly is the most affordable and beautiful health magazine, popular everywhere and praised by everyone. Recently, the company has received letters from readers both within and outside the city, stating that some individuals are falsely collecting money in the name of the magazine, falsely claiming to be sales representatives of the company, and defrauding readers of subscription fees for the monthly magazine. Upon investigation, all have been found to have been deceived. It is reported that the company, in addition to entrusting well-known and reliable bookstores and companies such as the Life Bookstore on Fourth Malu in the city to sell and subscribe on its behalf, currently does not authorize any individuals or specially appointed organizations to solicit subscriptions door-to-door. Furthermore, the company name is "Health World Society," and the address is "No. 14, Lane 214, Tongfu Road, Shanghai." It is also reported that the eighth issue of the monthly magazine, a special issue on health storage, is being typeset and is scheduled to be published on the 16th of this month. The retail price for each issue is one jiao in national currency. Direct subscriptions to the society's general distribution office for twelve issues per year, including postage within the country, cost only five jiao in national currency. Half-year subscriptions are not available.

Siming Hospital Adds Traumatology and Acupuncture Departments 153

The Siming Hospital on Aige Road in the legal district is a public hospital built with funds raised by fellow Ningbo natives in Shanghai. It is a large-scale institution and a leader among national medicine hospitals in Shanghai. Since the hospital's board of directors hired renowned physician Rong Mingshi as the hospital director and chief physician and Gu Jinhua as the director of general affairs, the internal operations have been continuously improved, and its reputation has been outstanding. Now, under Director Rong's leadership, the hospital has hired Lu Shikui, a renowned traumatologist from Ningbo, a member of society, to provide trauma care. Mr. Lu is skilled in treating various internal and external serious injuries and began providing treatment at the beginning of this month. Furthermore, starting on June 1st, the hospital has hired Sun Erkang, a veteran acupuncture specialist, to provide acupuncture treatment. From now on, the hospital will have a complete range of national medicine departments, greatly benefiting patients. Currently, the hospital treats over a hundred inpatients, with approximately two to three hundred outpatient visits per day. Therefore, the annual expenditure is at least fifty to sixty thousand yuan.

World Games Preliminaries and Sino-Western Confrontation - Seven National Records Broken 162

Three Track Events, Four Field Events, Plus Two Western Events - Only One Women's Event - Ten Events Continued Today

The World Games Track and Field Team Selection Competition was held at the Shen Garden yesterday afternoon. At the same time, a Sino-Western track and field confrontation was held to increase competitive interest. The elite of the country's track and field gathered to compete with the Shanghai Western expatriate athletes. Therefore, yesterday's situation and excitement were exceptionally enthusiastic. The audience reached four to five thousand people, and Mayor Wu also attended the event. Although the track and field finals were not as good as ideal, a total of seven national records were broken. In addition, the national records for the 400 meters and javelin were broken by Western athletes. The women's performance only held one item, the 100 meters, with Li Sen equaling the national record at 13.2 seconds. In addition to track and field, ten sports tests were added, with three participants. It will only be possible to complete the test this afternoon. Among the results, Jia Lianren's 1500 meters and Wang Shilin's triple jump were the most impressive. Liu Changchun's loss to Bowen in the 200 meters and Fu Baolu's departure from the field were the most disappointing. The results and situation are recorded below.

Seven New Records 163

Jia Lianren's 1500 Meters is Creditable - Huang Yingjie Overwhelms Lin Shaozhou in High Hurdles - Zhou Changxing and Guo Jie Unsuccessful

Yesterday, a total of seven new national records were set. In addition, the records for the 400 meters and javelin were broken by British soldier Bowen and Russian Kaczan. Among them, Jia Lianren's 1500 meters in 4 minutes and 11.1 seconds and Huang Yingjie's 15.7 seconds in the high hurdles, overwhelming Lin Shaozhou, were valuable gains. Zhou Changxing, who had a javelin of 53.85 meters, and Guo Jie, who had a discus of 41.13 meters, were both unsuccessful. Wang Shilin's triple jump was also not weak. Chen Baoqiu's long jump was far from the record he set in Beiping. The high jump and middle hurdles were also barely satisfactory. The seven new records are recorded as follows.

Discus - The first field event to end was the discus. With Guo Jie's rapid progress in the training class in Beiping, excellent results were expected. Unexpectedly, he repeatedly failed to achieve success. Leng Genpei, who lived in Shanghai, threw beyond 39 meters, overwhelming Guo Jie. Although both of their results broke Leng's national record of 37.85 meters, it was still far from Guo Jie's new record of 41.13 meters in Beiping. Named results are as follows:

Leng Peigen (China) 39.07

Guo Jie (China) 38.01

Kaczan (West) 37.49

Parker (West) 37.40

Shot Put - Five people participated. In the first throw, Chen Baoqiu got 12.88 meters, breaking his own national record of 12.69 meters, leading the group. Prokofiev also followed Chen with 12.61 meters. In the third throw, Pu got 12.66 meters. In the fifth throw, Kaczan made great progress, getting 12.58 meters. Parker also rose from fifth to fourth with 12.22 meters. Liu Furun's throw was invalidated due to stepping out of bounds after getting 12.13 meters in the second throw, and he was eliminated in fifth place. Chen's results were still far from the training class.

Javelin - Ten people participated in the competition. Our country's veterans Hao Chunde and Peng Yongxin, and the emerging star Zhou Changxing, all attended the battle. Unexpectedly, the three generals Peng, Hao, and Zhou were completely helpless. In the first throw, Nixon got more than 50 meters, Zhou got 48.31 meters, and Peng was close to 45 meters. After three throws, only Hao Chunde, Zhou Changxing, Wang Xuewu, Kaczan, and Nixon remained. Each throw progressed, and Kaczan surpassed Ni in the fifth attempt with 51.65 meters, surpassing our country's record. Hao also got 50.33 meters in the last attempt. Zhou never made progress and got fourth place.

Middle Hurdles - Although Cheng Jinguan's hurdle jumping technique is not refined and his posture is not high, he won the first place in the middle hurdles with his short-distance speed. 1500 Meters - In the 1500 meters final, Jia Lianren broke the national record with 4 minutes and 11.1 seconds, which was one of the most impressive events of yesterday's track and field. 400 Meters - Liu Changchun was defeated by Bowen in the 200 meters. In the 400 meters, Bowen exerted his authority again, overwhelming Dai Shuguo. Bowen's result was 50.2 seconds, which is rare in the country. Dai was 52.7 seconds, which was inferior to his national record of 51.6 seconds. He was five or six meters away from Bowen when he reached the finish line. Dong Shuzhao was third, and Li Yanxiang was fourth, which shows Bowen's strength. The point of Bowen's strength is that he has long legs and wide steps. It is also a surprise that there are such monsters among Westerners.

After Participating in the World Games, Jia Lianren Will Stay in Germany to Study Sports 164

Jia Lianren, who has repeatedly updated his national records in the middle distance, will stay in Germany to study sports after participating in the World Games this time, with a view to returning to China in three years.

Miscellaneous Notes on the Sino-Foreign Track and Field Competition 165

The Sino-Foreign competition, doubling as the national preliminary for the World Games track and field events, was held yesterday at the Shanghai Recreation Ground (申園). Because the Beijing training camp produced many new national and Far Eastern records, the people of Shanghai were captivated, with four to five thousand people visiting the recreation ground yesterday. There was also the McLeay military band and a phonograph, creating a very enthusiastic atmosphere, and people gradually dispersed only after the program was completed. However, some events that were expected to have good results were unexpectedly won by foreigners, which was a slight disappointment.

In the opening event, the 100 meters, Liu Changchun did not participate. The focus was on Chuan Jincheng and Cheng Jinguan. Due to false starts and the starting gun malfunctioning, multiple unsuccessful starts occurred before the race finally began on the fifth attempt. Chuan Jincheng won first place with a time of 10.9 seconds. He has plenty of strength and a good physique, but his sprint is weak, and his posture is not graceful.

The women's 100 meters was the only women's event yesterday, with only two participants: a blonde-haired woman, Meling Novska, and a Chinese athlete. At first, no one could tell who she was, but halfway through the race, it was recognized as the famous Miss Li Sen, number 111. Her momentum was quite impressive, leaving the Western woman more than 20 yards behind, and her time of 13.2 seconds equaled the national record. From then on, she dominated all the highest records in the women's triple race.

The first national record broken was in the 2:35 high hurdles, with an unexpected "upset." Huang Yingjie had never beaten Lin Shaozhou, but who would have thought that he would defeat Lin Shaozhou (the national record holder) with 15.7 seconds and set a new record? In the first six hurdles, Lin took the lead, and even at the last hurdle, he was on the balance line. Until the finish line, Huang's chest crossed Lin Shaozhou, securing first place. It seems that Lin's skill is also within the 16-second mark.

Bowen from the British army was very impressive, overshadowing both Liu Changchun and Dai Shukuo. In the 200 meters, Liu false-started by a step, and in the last 100 meters, Liu's steps seemed heavy. Bowen gradually took the lead, leaving Liu far behind, but his time of 22.7 seconds was only average. In the 400 meters, Bowen again showed his prowess. Although Dai Shukuo was also not bad, Bowen only took 50.2 seconds, far beyond what Dai could achieve. If our country's athletes had achieved this result, it would have been satisfactory.

In the discus and javelin, our country's athletes suffered unexpected defeats. Peng Yongxin and Zhou Changxing originally had skills exceeding 50 meters, but unexpectedly, Lao Peng failed twice and withdrew. Zhou only scored 48.31 meters. Old Hao (Chunde) still showed his strength, achieving 50.33 meters to get third place. The first and second places were both Westerners. Guo Jie once had a throw of 3.13 feet in the discus, and it was thought he would surely win the championship, but unexpectedly Leng Peigen, residing in Shanghai, beat Guo Jie with 39.07 meters, while Guo's was 38.01 meters. Although both were new national records, it cannot be considered satisfactory.

In the long jump, Wang Shilin once had an excellent result of 7.03 meters, but yesterday he only achieved 6.64 meters, getting third place. Ye Suian, the champion of the National Games, achieved 6.57 meters, a great disappointment. Zhang Jiakui won the championship with an ordinary score of 6.78 meters. The pole vault was the most interesting competition but was also very disappointing. Fu Baolu only tried once and stopped due to abdominal pain. Wang He once had a national record of 3.92 meters. In the competition against Abramov at the 3.48-meter mark, there was intense competition. Both barely managed to jump over it, but when deciding the ranking, Wang He only got second place.

The most satisfying were Jia Lianren's 1500 meters and Wang Shilin's triple jump, both of which had new records set. Jia had previously run 4 minutes and 13 seconds, but yesterday he shortened it by nearly two seconds. Wang's triple jump of 14.36 meters was also very commendable. Situ Guang made a comeback and was still able to maintain a skill above 14 meters, which is truly not easy. Jia's 800 meters time of 2 minutes and 3.6 seconds was far from the 2 minutes and 0.3 seconds he achieved in the competition against Tianjin.

In the shot put, Chen Baoqiu scored 12.88 meters, which is also a national record, but not his best performance. Liu Furun once had 12.95 meters in the competition against Tianjin, but yesterday he didn't even place, getting fifth with 12.13 meters. Wu Bixian's high jump of 1.85 meters was not bad. He failed three attempts at 1.875 meters.

The 400-meter hurdles was truly an "upset," with no satisfactory talent emerging. Cheng Yuguan took a chance and broke the national record with 58.3 seconds. However, his posture of hooking his back foot under his buttocks while clearing the hurdle still remains unchanged. If he attends the World Games, will foreigners laugh at China for not having a coach?

The 10,000 meters was dull because the old man from Shanxi did not come to Shanghai. Liu Changchun also did not participate in the two relay races. With such a well-organized lineup, no good results were achieved, which was very disappointing. The baton exchange was too untrained. It not only failed to save time but also delayed it. The American relay teams often do not consist of formal competitors, yet their results repeatedly set new world records. The art of baton exchange is truly too scientific.

Yesterday, in addition to the formal program, there was a sudden impromptu decathlon test, with Zhou Changxing, Cheng Mengping, and Zhang Lingjia participating. Is it necessary for our country's decathlon performance to also attend the World Games? The saying "talent as the standard" is difficult to explain.

Overall, yesterday's results were generally not bad. There were unexpected gains and unexpected failures. What kind of perspective will the selection committee use for selection? Sending twelve track and field athletes is not a small number. Sending more athletes is not necessarily a meritorious deed. It seems more practical to hire a few foreign coaches to guide them. China is not lacking in sports talent!

Bowen, first in the 200 and 400 meters (Lin She photo)

Liu Changchun's Decline 166

Defeated by Bowen in the 200 meters, his performance was mediocre.

Liu Changchun, our country's first and only sprinter to attend the World Games, did not show his face in the Beijing training camp due to a leg injury. Yesterday, he only participated in the 200 meters event, unexpectedly being defeated by the British soldier Bowen, whose time was 22.7 seconds, which was quite average. Liu was about four or five yards behind, estimated to be above 23 seconds. Observing his steps in the last 100 meters, they were quite heavy. His leg injury should be taken seriously, and the lack of practice has contributed to this. Fu Baolu only tried once in the pole vault and gave up due to abdominal pain, which was very disappointing. It is regrettable that Jia Lianren failed to set a new record in the 800 meters. Wang Shilin was also unsuccessful in the long jump. The other results were mediocre.

The long jump performance was mediocre, and the expectation of a new record became a bubble. The results of the top four are as follows:

Zhang Jiakui (China) 6.78

Okubo (West) 6.67

Wang Shilin (China) 6.64

Ye Suian (China) 6.57

Wang Shilin, who previously set a new national record of 7.01 meters, had no good performance after achieving 6.64 meters on his second attempt.

800 meters: The 800-meter final was highly anticipated by the crowd due to Jia Lianren's presence. Jia had achieved a time of 2 minutes and 0.3 seconds in Beijing, so there was hope that he could break into the 2-minute mark. Unfortunately, he arrived from Jinan late last night and did not have enough rest, so although the championship was not in question, his time was only 2 minutes and 3.6 seconds. In the first 300 meters, Jia's speed was very average, and he only increased his pace after 300 meters. Reaching the finish line, he could only equal the record. Li Shiming and the Westerner Aflei competed fiercely, with Li only finishing second by a shoulder, about thirty or more meters behind Jia. Zhao Miaogen was fourth.

100 meters: The men's 100-meter final was the opening act, with three participants from both China and the West. The Chinese were Chuan Yucheng, Cheng Jinguan, and Zhao Bingheng. Liu Changchun rested for the 100 meters to fully focus on the 200 meters. The Westerners were all mediocre. After the gun was fired and recalled, they finally started. Chuan Jincheng took the lead, with a very fast start. Behind Chuan was Cheng, followed by Zhao and the three Westerners. After 50 meters, Cheng Jinguan's speed increased sharply, charging forward, almost alongside Chuan. It was a very dangerous situation, but upon reaching the finish line, Cheng was second by a chest. Chuan's time was 10.9 seconds, which was better than usual. Zhao Bingheng was third, and the Englishman Bellay was fourth.

200 meters: Liu Changchun put all his efforts into the 200-meter final. Liu only attended the first test in Beijing, achieving 22.9 seconds, and then retired for rest. His recent strength was therefore of great interest. However, the result yesterday was that he was defeated by the British soldier Bowen. Bowen's time was 22.7 seconds, and Liu was about three meters behind, around 23 seconds. The failure of Liu's 200 meters, which was a sure thing, in the domestic first competition was quite surprising to the three thousand spectators. Bowen was in the innermost lane, and Liu was in the middle. After turning at the 100-meter mark, Bowen emerged, overtaking Liu after 150 meters and sprinting to the end. Third was Sidney Qinggu, and fourth was Stettou. Bowen was unmatched in height, with large and fast strides, making Liu no match for him.

10,000 meters: The 10,000 meters was one of the least interesting events yesterday. The Shanxi athletes were only seen by name and not in person. There were five participants, and only three finished the entire course to the end. The first was Wang Zhenglin, the second was the Japanese Murakami, and the third was Zhang Liang. The results were mediocre, 35 minutes and 16.6 seconds. Murakami was 150 meters behind Wang, and Zhang Liang was 300 meters behind Wang.

Two Relay Races: The closing acts, the 400-meter relay and the 1600-meter relay, were both won by the Chinese team. Although both teams were made up of star players, the results were mediocre and unexciting due to the lack of baton exchange skills. The 400 meters was 45.8 seconds. The order of the runners was as follows: first leg Zhao Bingheng, second leg Cheng Jinguan, third leg Huang Yingjie, and final leg Chuan Jincheng. It can be said that the baton exchange between Cheng and Huang was the most disjointed. The 1600 meters was 3 minutes and 38.6 seconds. The order of the runners was as follows: first leg Dong Shuzhao, second leg Li Yanxiang, third leg Jia Lianren, and final leg Dai Shukuo. Neither broke the record. The Englishman Bowen and Liu Changchun did not participate.

Pole Vault: Fu Baolu only tried once and gave up due to abdominal pain. Only Wang He and Abramov competed, greatly reducing the interest. The two struggled for a long time, barely clearing 3.48 meters, tying for first place. In the deciding round, Wang He fell behind.

Women's 100 Meters: Li Sen Equals National Record 167

A total of nine female athletes from the Chinese team registered, but none of them participated. Only Li Sen attended. Only Meling Novska participated from the Western team, so all the other competitions were announced to be canceled. Only Li and Mei performed a 100-meter exhibition race. It started at 2:30. As soon as the starting gun fired, Li Sen sprinted forward, and Mei Ling could not keep up. After 50 meters, she was already two meters behind. Li made a final effort to sprint, reaching the finish line, leaving Mei Ling about three meters behind. The time was 13.2 seconds, equaling the national record of Jiao Yulian and Zhang Jieqiong.
