— The Municipal Boy Scouts Held a Grand Review Yesterday Morning, Practiced Emergency Drills in the Afternoon, and Held a Bonfire Party for Entertainment in the Evening

The boy scouts from various primary and secondary schools and social organizations in the city set off from their original locations on the 6th, advancing towards the city center. After arriving, they set up camps and pitched tents. The administrative area was transformed into a military area. A grand review was held in the stadium yesterday morning, and an emergency period performance was given in the afternoon, suddenly changing the atmosphere and creating an unusually tense atmosphere. There was a bonfire party in the evening for entertainment. The details are recorded as follows:

Camp Inspection: The total number of young children participating in this event reached over seven thousand. The camping area in front of the Municipal Government lasted for three days and nights. The camping area was green with grass, and the tents were scattered like stars. Banners and flags fluttered, bright and dazzling. Bugles sounded from time to time, and the sound of drums created a solemn atmosphere, resembling a battle array.

Review Ceremony: The grand review was held at the Municipal Stadium yesterday at 9 a.m. The chairman, vice-chairman, reviewing officers, all general meeting officials, and Chinese and foreign guests were seated on the western command platform. After the boy scouts being reviewed entered, cannons were fired and flags were raised. First, the chairman and vice-chairman gave instructions, and then the review began. After the review, there was cheering, and the ceremony ended. The reviewed teams withdrew from the venue in an orderly manner, with strict discipline, a good order, and better results than in the past.

Number of Participants: Those who participated in the review ceremony included Chairman Wu Tiecheng, Vice-Chairmen Tong Hangbai and Pan Gongzhan, Municipal Public Security Bureau Director Cai Jingjun, Municipal Council Speaker Wang Xiaolai, US Commercial Counselor Arnold, Municipal Government Secretaries Zhang Tingrong and Tang Shihuang, Municipal Stadium Director Shao Rugan, and the general meeting's officials Leng Xueqiao, Shen Yu, Xi Yutong, and Xia Huanxin, as well as more than 10,000 boy scouts from the city.

Assembly and Entry: At 8 a.m., the boy scouts separately assembled in front of each camp and marched to the stadium. By 9 a.m., the teams had assembled outside the stadium. The general commander Sun Yixin issued an order to advance, and each team and troop entered the venue in four columns, following the track in a large circle. The military band led the way, and each team was led by a dark green team flag, which looked like a yellowish-brown wreath from afar.

Airplane Circling: At 9 a.m. on this day, the Shanghai Boy Scouts airplane circled low over the city center and around the stadium, and then ascended directly into the sky, continuing to perform various maneuvers for 15 minutes before flying away. Around 11 a.m., when the cheering ceremony was over, it flew back, circling several times and performing various maneuvers before leaving.

Firing Cannons and Raising Flags: After the teams were lined up in the venue, the meeting was announced to begin. First, firecrackers were set off, and then the flag-raising ceremony was held. While singing the flag-raising song, General Commander Sun Yixin issued the order to stand at attention, and all the boy scouts stood at attention and performed the baton salute. The team leaders and coaches performed the hand salute, and the team flag bearers tilted the team flags forward by 30 degrees.

The Mayor of Wu is on the right corner of the Boy Scout Meeting Flag Raising (Wang Kai photo)

Chairman's Report: After the ceremony, Chairman Wu Tiecheng gave an opening speech, which read: "All boy scouts, directors, distinguished guests, and boy scouts: Today is the opening ceremony of the Shanghai Boy Scouts Seventh General Assembly. We have 15,000 boy scouts in Shanghai, and those who participated today account for half of them. The number of participants in this event is unprecedented in the history of Shanghai Boy Scout General Assemblies. The organization of the team is also unprecedented. With so many people participating, yet so orderly and full of energy, the citizens of Shanghai see that, I believe they are not only happy and delighted, but also that they have an even greater belief in the future of China. What is this greater belief? It is that they believe that there is hope for the future of China. Our China has now reached a very dangerous juncture, and the Chinese nation is now suffering a great threat. Therefore, we must now seek survival, and the basic task of seeking survival is to build a nation. What kind of nation should we build? We must build a nation of the Three Principles of the People. Building a nation depends on the people. We must have good citizens in order to build a good nation. Only a good nation can be strong, and only a strong nation can survive. But how can we be good citizens? We must be able to 'cultivate oneself, manage one's family, govern the country, and bring peace to the world.' Cultivating oneself, managing one's family, governing the country, and bringing peace to the world is the highest political philosophy in China. If each of us can do 'cultivate oneself, manage one's family, govern the country, and bring peace to the world,' we can be considered good citizens. Good citizens can build a good nation, and a good nation can seek survival. But how can we train each citizen so that they can do 'cultivate oneself, manage one's family, govern the country, and bring peace to the world?' We must start training from children. Children are the future masters of China. Today we train children, and we are training the future masters of China. The future masters of China will bear the great responsibility of revitalizing the Chinese nation. The best way to train children is through Boy Scout education, because the organization and training of Boy Scouts are the best methods for training children. Since the children of China today are the future masters of China, the purpose of the Chinese Boy Scouts is to 'develop children's ability to do things, cultivate good habits, so that they are noble in character, rich in common sense, and healthy in body, becoming youths with both wisdom, benevolence, and courage, to build a nation of the Three Principles of the People, and to achieve world harmony.' We also take China's inherent virtues, loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, and peace, as the highest principles of training Boy Scouts, so it can be said that Boy Scout training is instructing us on the principles of being and doing, which is also our highest ideal. We hope that the children of China today will use Boy Scout training as a guideline for our future actions, and Boy Scout training as our highest and purest ideal. Therefore, today we hold the opening ceremony of the Shanghai Boy Scouts Seventh General Assembly. We not only want to review the achievements of all the Boy Scouts in Shanghai, but also want to awaken Shanghai society and the parents of Shanghai to know the meaning of the Boy Scouts, and to dedicate their children to the country and society, to receive Boy Scout training, to promote Boy Scout training and movements. We hope that after this year's review, when we hold another review next year, the results will be better than this year. We cannot but hope that our Shanghai Boy Scouts will abide by the Boy Scout rules and oaths, strive to be good Boy Scouts, and prepare to be good citizens in the future, to take on the great responsibility of revitalizing the Chinese nation."

Start of the Review: After the chairman's report, the review began. Chairman Wu Tiecheng, along with all the reviewing officers, went down to the west command platform and to the center of the venue, inspecting the teams along the way. When the reviewing personnel went down, the general commander issued an order to stand at attention. When the reviewing personnel passed each team, the team leader issued an order to salute. The Boy Scouts performed the baton salute, the team leader performed the hand salute, and the team flag was tilted forward by 30 degrees. Everyone watched until the reviewing personnel had passed, and then the team leader issued an order to end the salute. After the reviewing personnel had inspected the area for a week, they returned to the command platform and continued to perform basic movements. The general commander issued the orders: Stand at attention, Right dress, Eyes front, Right face, About face, Left face, About face, Shoulder arms, Order arms, At ease. Finally, it was the marching style. The general commander issued the orders: Stand at attention, Right face, Shoulder arms, Forward, march. The military music began to play, marching around the track. Each team passed in front of the command platform, and the team leader issued an order to Eyes right. The Boy Scouts looked to the right, passing with a parade step, until the last row had passed the command platform, and then issued the Eyes front order. The steps were very orderly, and the reviewing officers applauded to welcome them. The entire group circled the venue once and lined up in front of the command platform, standing in formation.

Instructions from Tong and Pan: After the review, Tong Hangbai gave instructions, briefly mentioning that the annual Boy Scout review is being held here today. The number of participants this time is greater than in previous years, and the curriculum has also increased compared to previous years. This cannot but be said to be a significant improvement. For example, in the curriculum, there is this time an emergency period exercise and labor service. The former is for the sake of the country, and the latter is for the sake of society. In other words, the Boy Scout community today has a further understanding of the country and society, but in the future, we should also pay attention to the advancement of technology, in order to achieve the purpose of perfection. Then Pan Gongzhan gave instructions, briefly saying that he is responsible for education in this city, and is very pleased to see that all the Boy Scouts are energetic and in good order today. As for Boy Scout training, attention should be paid to three aspects: Brain training, that is, to enable each person to fully use their brains, increase their knowledge, and be able to distinguish right from wrong; Heart training, that is, to cultivate in each person the concepts of "brightness," "conscience," "universal love," and "benevolence and righteousness"; Hand training, that is, to do a good deed every day. In this way, one can conform to the three virtues of "wisdom," "benevolence," and "courage."

Singing and Welcoming: After the instructions, everyone sang the Boy Scout song, and then everyone shouted "Move, move, move, Alert, alert, alert, Shanghai Boy Scouts, Boy Scouts, Strive forward, Revitalizing China is our responsibility, Boom, boom, boom, Clang, clang, clang, Chinese Boy Scouts, Boy Scouts, Long live." Then the ceremony ended.

Emergency Exercises: Starting at 1:30 p.m., the emergency exercises began. The general headquarters was set up on the west command platform of the Municipal Stadium, with a large flag hanging to identify it. At 1:30 p.m., the general headquarters issued a general alarm using the sound system. Everyone made preparations. At 2:00 p.m., enemy aircraft were detected entering the front line, so the second alarm was issued, and each group departed for activities. The exercises were divided into the communications group, commanded by Gong Jingzeng; the transportation group, commanded by Xu Guozhi; the anti-poisoning group, commanded by Za Lie; the engineering group, commanded by Sun Yiming; the rescue group, commanded by Xie Yanbo; the relief group, commanded by Sun Yixin; and the fire-fighting group, commanded by Shen Yu. It was not completed until 5:00 p.m.

Today's Order: This morning, a memorial week will be held in the stadium, followed by a course competition. This afternoon, the course competition will continue. The courses include rescue, surveying, mapping, knotting, cooking, semaphore, and other items. There will also be a talent show in the evening.

Spring and Autumn

Gleanings 173

— (Shi Gandang)

As foreign aggression intensifies and national crises deepen, a certain bookstore publishes books like "A Hundred Days to Master X Language" and "Basic X Language," even going so far as to advertise them extensively, saying: "Literate compatriots, hurry and learn X Language. The greater purpose is to serve the nation (?) and protect the family, and the smaller purpose is to make a name for yourself..." If everyone holds this view, it would be unreasonable for China not to perish.

I remember a certain teacher at an X school saying: Instead of students striving to pursue women, they should bury themselves in hard work. Once they become famous, they won't need to pursue the women; the women will come seeking them. I think everything is like this. Instead of seeking help from others, it's better to make others seek help from you, but the difficulty lies in how to make others seek help from you.

An old woman at home went to a temple to burn incense and fell! She broke her hand, but blamed herself for somehow offending the Bodhisattva, leading to this misfortune. Hearing this, I felt both amused and pitying.

When you are about to do something to someone, you must first put yourself in the other person's position and think about it. For example, when you are unhappy, you arbitrarily scold servants, but if you put yourself in the servant's position, can you endure being scolded for no reason? In this way, the anger in your heart will immediately dissipate. I often use this method to curb momentary anger.

Early Summer, in the Style of a Young Woman 174

— Zhou Xian

Summer is a gradually maturing young woman. Although not as seductive as a girl in early spring, it resembles a mature young woman, displaying the fullness of muscles and lines, no longer containing full childishness.

Indeed, early summer can be described as a girl nearing twenty, inherently pregnant with a kind of great fervor and strength.

In the uncertain atmosphere of a spring filled with sunshine and shade, I was huddled in a pigeon cage-like room. By chance, and quite suddenly, in the bright sunlight of an early summer day, I walked to the suburbs, which was truly beyond expectations. Green grass covered the ugly mud, as if covered with a blanket. Looking at it, it seemed completely inelastic, like a soft quilt.

Sure enough, the sunlight also seemed to emit a different kind of brilliance than what I saw two months ago. When it shone on my body, I felt that my thin jacket was already a bit too thick.

A few faded peach blossoms still lingered on the peach branches, but plum fruits as large as longans had already grown on the plum branches. The willow branches were also wrapped in a layer of green clothing, extending out from the corner of the fence outside the village, brushing against the brims of pedestrians' hats, so gentle, so affectionate, so captivating and memorable.

On the surface of the quiet little pond, large and small, round duckweeds floated, seeming to cover the pond surface with a quilt printed with patterns designed by artists, rich in artistic meaning. The grass on the banks of the pond seemed to be contending with the duckweed, vying to see who was a more vivid and verdant green. However, a few wild rose bushes by the stone steps trembled with a few round, carmine flowers, constantly nodding to the green grass and the green duckweed, as if smiling. Although the surroundings of the small pond were so quiet that only one or two bees occasionally buzzed by, and one or two small fish occasionally jumped in the duckweed, making a sound of splashing water that broke the silence, the surroundings of this small pond were filled with the vitality and vigor of duckweed, grass, wild roses, and all living things.

Unmarried girls are indeed lovable, but mature girls with beautiful lines have a different kind of charm. This is the unique beauty of early summer.

The Banana Tree Turns Green 175

— Shu Fan

As the gardens enter summer, all the greenery turns lush, vitality surging, making one feel refreshed. And the banana tree, with its fresh green color, brings coolness to the window screen, especially suitable for evoking reveries. When the morning dew first nourishes it, and the breeze caresses the eaves, one sees it standing tall and upright, like a humble maid offering her services, dressed in a green cloth skirt. Contemplating it always brings great joy. At midday, when it is slightly warm and the phoenix tail fern is quiet, the gentle breeze wafts through, bringing countless coolness, as if many young maids are holding green gauze fans. Then again, it seems self-admiring. By evening, when the sunset is intoxicating and the rosy clouds are faint, it is as if someone is swaying, holding a green curtain, surpassing Xie Daoyun in elegance. All these are my joyful reflections on a cluster of banana trees. As for moonlit nights, when the wind's murmur has not ceased, it resembles a recluse, sighing with ups and downs, then I can't help but wring my hands all night, pacing restlessly. Sometimes, in a curtain of drizzle, the bean lamp casts a sickly green glow, and hearing the tree's whispered complaints, it's like a grieving widow on the Cold Food Festival, weeping at her grave, even soaking through my spring clothes, sobbing uncontrollably. A small thing can move people so deeply, hence my singular devotion.

I remember my father telling me a story when I was a child: "In the past, Huai Su sat in the Green Heaven Monastery. He was poor and had no paper, so he used ten thousand banana leaves to write on, and made great progress. My son, you don't have to worry about paper and pens, so I hope you cherish them!" At that time, a crescent moon hung on the bean trellis, thin clouds were often cut by it, and shooting stars and fireflies were mixed in a chaotic shooting, my eyes followed them, my heart was amazed, I responded casually, without time to remember. Twenty years have passed in a flash, my father is already old and frail, although I labor with the inkstone, I have only made spring earthworm and autumn snake-like progress, without the slightest improvement. Every time I write a letter home, I still open it before sending it, not knowing where to start to express my shame.

At the age of ten, I studied at Hu's Suizhen Residence. My cousin, Ya Xue, was the most intelligent. Her essays and antithetical couplets were unmatched. She especially loved reciting poems from the Thousand-Character Classic. At sunset, after school was dismissed, I often saw her sitting under a banana tree, reciting a volume of poetry. Azure clouds streamed down on her pink collar and skirt, creating a unique and enchanting scene. She was absorbed in contemplation during meals, but when my cousin coughed, she turned red and fled back home, not daring to look directly for three days. This scene is vivid, as if it were yesterday. In late spring, I revisited the old school. The banana trees had grown taller and more luxuriant. I heard that A Ya had been a widow for over a year, how sad indeed!

From childhood, I was most cherished by my aunt, who kept me warm and comfortable, like a loving mother. When I was eleven, my aunt suddenly passed away from illness. It was the height of summer. The coffin was covered with banana leaves. I wailed until noon, my eyes blurred, only vaguely seeing my aunt lying in green clouds, still hoping that she would get up, pat my head, and give me biscuits. When I realized that my aunt would never return, I stamped my feet and cried loudly. Since then, every year when the banana leaves turn green, I see my aunt's kind face faintly emerging from them.

The Phoenixes Switch Nests 176

— By Zhang Henshui

Chapter Two: Fragrant Grass and Beautiful Woman, Subtle Waves Gently Support Her; Small Building, Bright Moon, Warm Dreams Begin

Wu Ma poured a cup of tea and placed it on the table, smiling, "Miss, you haven't smiled all day. It's like this book is a joyous event come to earth. You smiled as soon as you received it." Menglan said, "I don't have anything to be happy about right now, so I'm just using books to relieve boredom. Once the books arrive, I'll finish them in a day and a night, and then I'll have to wait another half a month. I'm happy for a moment when I receive the book, isn't it natural?" As she spoke, she reached out to flip through the magazine, first looking at the table of contents for the current issue. Among them was a line that read, "A Love That Can't Be," followed by the name Zhang Litian. She couldn't help but laugh and say, "This issue has another one of his tragic love stories." Wu Ma was startled, looking at her and saying, "Miss, what are you talking about?" Menglan raised her head, but her face turned red, smiling, "You don't know, I'm talking about something in the book. You wouldn't understand." Hearing that it was something she couldn't understand, Wu Ma saw no need to ask further and went downstairs. Menglan wiped the table clean and then spread the book open to read. Flipping past the table of contents, she saw a page with photos of the magazine's authors. The third photo was of a young man in his early twenties, exactly like the young man she had met at Yuhuatai today. She couldn't help but stare fixedly, gazing at him for a long time. After about ten minutes, she nodded to herself, muttering, "I guessed right, it really is him." Then she covered the book and pondered again. She felt as if the young man at Yuhuatai, with a smile, was standing in front of her desk. "Oh! I'm bewitched!" She propped her head and looked at the willow trees outside the window, trying to calm herself and cast aside this terrible illusion. But the willow branches were swaying in the wind, very much like the hem of the young man's clothes at Yuhuatai this afternoon, fluttering in the wind. She didn't dare to look out the window anymore and instead turned back to the table, flipping open the book. The story, "A Love That Can't Be," was published on the first page of the magazine, so she saw it as soon as she opened it. The story began:

"One evening, on a night of bright stars and a brilliant moon, autumn clouds floated across the sky, thin as silk gauze. Qin Yizhi and his intimate friend Lin Yinghua were drinking in a small room in a Mingxia Lane tavern. The bright lights shone, radiating charm, reflecting on Lin Yinghua's cheeks. A shy blush surged, reaching her temples, like rose petals. Once the wine was poured, she raised her cup and toasted, saying, 'May the joy of our meetings remain with us in our years of melancholy, with more laughter and less tears.'"

Seeing this, Menglan couldn't help but mutter to herself, "This is another soul-stirring story. This Mr. Zhang seems to have a grudge against the readers, determined to force all their tears out before he's satisfied." (31)

Miscellaneous Talk

Rambling Chat on Goldfish 177

— Wu Jiren

I haven't written about goldfish for months, but I am constantly surrounded by them. Every day, countless small fish are born, impossible to count. This year the weather is not good, and many hobbyists have reported fish diseases. This is partly due to careless water changes and partly due to the rainy weather.

It is easier to treat goldfish whose heads and tails have white patches. You can buy borax water at the pharmacy and mix it with warm water in the fish tank (warm water is water that has been boiled and left to cool for a week, not freshly boiled water). Take the fish out and put it in the bucket, and gently rub the white patches with your hand. The white rot will come off layer by layer. For mild cases, one bath is enough to cure them, and for severe cases, two or three times will be enough. It has been proven effective repeatedly.

If you want to get new and unusual varieties of goldfish, it is undoubtedly important to mix the breeds during mating. However, you must first pay attention to when they are carrying eggs (I seem to have mentioned this in a previous article, specifically in issue 37 last winter, because winter turns to spring, and fish's spring instincts are activated.) Then, when they are spawning, make them mix and chase each other, so you can hopefully get something. It is generally not advisable to mix too many types. For example, mixing "dragon eye" and "bubble eye" gives "dragon eye bubble eye," and mixing "celestial eye" and "bubble eye" gives "celestial bubble eye." It is definitely not advisable to mix bubble eye and "black moor" or "purple goldfish," hoping to create a "black celestial bubble eye" etc. You can only select one out of a hundred from this year's mixed breeds, choosing those with a straight head and eyes, or those with larger bubbles, and you will get "celestial bubble eyes" and "dragon eye bubble eyes." If you want to get blue or purple celestial bubble eyes and dragon eye bubble eyes, you must try again next spring using the same method. We only seek new varieties, not quantity, and a few will not be difficult to obtain.

The sex life of goldfish has some new discoveries. Recently, on humid and hot mornings and after changing to fresh water, you can be sure that there will be several tanks spawning. However, in the same tank, on the same day that new water is changed, one tank will be vigorously chasing each other, fighting over algae, neglecting everything to spawn, while in another tank, the males and females will be listless and motionless. I was curious and put a male fish into the spawning tank. In no time, it joined the fray, chasing tirelessly. I also put a female fish in there to test it. The males, seeing another object of interest, chased each other even more, vying and pursuing, not leaving for a moment, trying to get them to spawn at the same time. I then took a pair that were vigorously chasing each other and put them in a tank that was not spawning, but they also became listless as if nothing had happened. From this, it can be seen that spawning in goldfish is partly based on sexual arousal and partly related to the water. However, overly mature female fish, with abdomens as big as drums, swim awkwardly, and often release eggs among the algae without being chased by male fish, but these lone eggs may not hatch.

A few days ago, a friend came to my farm in Caohejing and visited me, talking about how he wanted to give me two male pearl goldfish, saying that the pearl goldfish he kept at home had big bellies but no sign of chasing, fearing they might have trouble spawning and die from bloating, so he had to get two male fish. I laughed and replied, noting that the mature female fish I had could lay eggs without being chased, so the bloating theory could be dismissed, but without male fish, there would definitely be no baby fish.

Small Spring and Autumn Weekly

Guizhou Folk Song 179

— (Egret Gentleman)

Waiting for my love to return, waiting for him, night after night, guarding my empty boudoir.

Could it be that he has found love in another land?

Forgetting his old mother and abandoning his beautiful wife. A bright red floral cloth, brand new, I'll give it to my little sister to make an apron; one day when she marries to the north of the mountain, she can wear the skirt and remember the person who gave it to her.

Xukou 180

— Wang Zhiqin

Suzhou, famous for its beautiful scenery, is full of famous mountains and scenic spots. Xukou is also one of the famous scenic spots in Wudi. It is located near Muzhen, and is the main route to Taihu Lake. Xushan is to its south and Xiangshan is to its north. Xukou is located between the two mountains. Outside the mouth, the water connects with the sky, with silver waves, and inside the mouth, the scenery is secluded and beautiful, like an absolutely beautiful woman. There are no great buildings or important people's villas here. All there are are bamboo houses, willow pavilions, small boats and light gulls, flowing with the waves. However, tourists who see this natural water village map can't help but feel a sense of detachment. I hope that the elegant scholars who travel to Suzhou's Yan Hill will also take a trip to Xukou in the fishing village. If due to time constraints, they cannot have both, then abandoning the former and traveling to Xukou alone is also worthwhile.

Ye Tianshi 181

— Lanshan

Ye Tianshi from Suzhou was a famous doctor during the Yongzheng and Qianlong periods of the Qing Dynasty. He had a sharp mind and deep understanding of medicine, but was lazy and fond of playing, and did not often make house calls, earning him a reputation for arrogance. He often used strange and unusual methods to treat people's illnesses. He was skilled in treating all kinds of diseases. It is said that he studied with seventeen teachers in seven years. If a certain teacher had a specialty in a certain disease, he would master their method before leaving, so the essence of all schools was gathered in one person, and his great reputation was not accidental. Later, he cured the dangerous illness of Zhang Zhenren of Longhu Mountain and was given the title of Heavenly Doctor Star. The gentleman was also generous, and he always gave medicine and treatment to the poor and sick, saving countless lives. Even today, people still praise him.

The gentleman's mother once suffered from a feverish disease. He diagnosed and treated her himself, but observing her pulse, it seemed like a cold syndrome, and he dared not prescribe medicine hastily. He paced the courtyard in the evening, saying to himself, "If she were someone else's mother, I would use Baihu Decoction!" His words were heard by an old man from the neighboring family, also a doctor. The next day, the old man visited Tianshi, pretending to want to examine his mother. After examining her pulse, he prescribed Baihu Decoction, and she recovered miraculously after one dose. The old doctor's fame greatly increased. In fact, it was still Tianshi's achievement.

Small Statistics on Lost Territory 182

— (Wu Hou)

From September 18th to now, our country has lost more than eight million square li of territory! More than 1.5 million square li more than the total territory lost by the Qing government in recent centuries!

If the lost territory is compared to the provinces, it is equivalent to: Seven Sichuans; Twelve Guangdongs; Thirteen Hunan; Fourteen Shaanxi; Fifteen Hubei; Sixteen Henans; Seventeen Shanxis; Eighteen Shandong; Nineteen Anhui; Twenty-three Fujian; Twenty-seven Jiangsu; Twenty-eight Zhejiang.

If the lost territory is compared to foreign countries, it is even more shocking. It is equivalent to the sum of the land area of eleven countries: Japan, England, France, Germany, Italy, Austria, Hungary, Belgium, Netherlands, Denmark, and Sweden! In other words, it can also be said to be equal to: Four Frances; Five Germanys; Six Japans; Ten Englands; Sixty Switzerlands; Seventy Netherlands; Eighty Belgiums.

Page 15

Economic Special Issue

The New Development of China's Monetary Policy 183

— Wang Lie Wang

Since the U.S. President announced the silver purchasing policy in December 1933, the world silver price has been entirely controlled by the United States. Last year, from April to May, the United States heavily purchased silver in the London market, causing silver prices to soar, reaching a high of over 33 pence in May. China was finally forced to abandon the silver standard on November 4 and implement currency management, with the Central Bank of China, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications buying and selling foreign exchange without restrictions to stabilize foreign exchange rates. However, after mid-December of that year, the United States stopped purchasing silver in the London market; China's currency system again felt a great threat. According to general opinion, the foreign exchange rate of the new currency system was pegged at one shilling and two and a half pence, and its parity with the silver reserve should be seventeen and seventy-five pence, the calculation method as follows:

? Pence = Standard Ounce of Silver

Standard Ounce of Pure Silver 23.49348 grams = One Yuan Silver Coin

That is to say, only when the value of each ounce of new standard silver in London is 17.75 pence, the actual value of one yuan silver coin is equivalent to one shilling and two and a half pence. If the London silver price falls below 17.75 pence, it will not be easy to maintain the foreign exchange rate of one shilling and two and a half pence. Because Article 4 of the legal tender decree announced by the Ministry of Finance on November 4 last year stipulates: "All silver firms, shops, and other public and private institutions or individuals holding silver standard coins or other silver coins, raw silver, etc., should, from November 4, hand them over to the Issuance Reserve Management Committee or its designated bank for exchange into legal tender. In addition to silver standard coins being exchanged for legal tender at face value, the remaining silver will be exchanged according to the actual amount of pure silver contained." In this way, if the London silver price falls below 17.75 pence, overseas silver will flow into China again, exchanged for legal tender according to the actual amount of pure silver contained, and then the three banks will purchase shillings with legal tender, and the foreign exchange reserve of the three banks can be exhausted in an instant. I believe that this danger can still be avoided. Since China has actually stopped the silver standard, the Ministry of Finance can revise the previous decree if necessary, and can set another market price and purchase at price, so that those who take advantage have no profit to make, then this danger can be avoided. What is worrying is that the international balance of payments is still in a reverse state (according to the Bank of China's 20th-year report and G. Edward's estimate of the international balance of payments, the export of silver and gold still occupies an important position). In the future, the maintenance of foreign exchange reserves still requires the sale of silver in exchange. If the silver price falls, then we must exchange a large amount of silver for a small amount of foreign currency. If the silver price falls, then we must exchange a large amount of silver for a small amount of foreign currency. Today, one yuan silver coin can be exchanged for one shilling and a half pence, and in the future, it may be necessary to exchange one and a half yuan for it. Therefore, the foreign exchange reserve will inevitably feel weak. If it reaches the point of desperation, then we can only lower the foreign exchange rate to protect ourselves, and the stability of the exchange rate will fail as a result. The danger of falling silver prices lies in this and not in that. However, many commentators say that from now on, judging from the actual situation of silver supply and demand, it should hover around 19 pence, and will not fall again. How it will be in the end, I am afraid it is not easy to predict.

Today, the only buyer of silver is the United States. In the past, China was a demander of silver. Since abandoning the silver standard last year, it has changed into a supplier of silver. However, China is restricted by the 1933 Silver Agreement and cannot sell in the London market during the agreement period (expiring in 1938). Even without this restriction, if the United States stops purchasing silver, the London silver market will never improve, and China is also unwilling to sell at low prices. In order to find a way out for the silver reserve, it is necessary to consult with the United States. The United States' use of the silver purchase policy originally had the intention of manipulating China's currency system, so that China had to associate with it in order to expand the scope of the dollar group. Since Chen Guangfu and others went to the United States to negotiate a currency agreement with the US financial authorities, both China and the United States were tight-lipped at first. Only recently have various news spread. US Senator King declared that the Chinese representatives went to Washington to purchase silver from the United States. This news was quite surprising to all parties. Since King is a representative of the silver faction, it is also possible that he said this to confuse the public. All parties may as well listen to it for the time being. China feels that there is no way to dispose of the silver reserve, so how can there be any reason to buy silver from the United States again? Later, it was rumored that China would soon mint silver dollars, with the intention of restoring the silver standard, which is even more absurd. As the Bank of China report said: "At this time of rising and falling silver prices, and the disputes over the domestic economy, unless most countries believe that silver still has a use value in the currency system, considering the restoration of the silver standard would be a major mistake." Recently, it has been rumored that the government will recast one yuan silver coins, with the size and color only equal to one-third of the original silver dollar; and it is said that this recasting is equivalent to devaluation. The Minister of Finance has already published a statement in the newspaper to correct it. Regarding the minting of silver coins, G. Edward, who has always been valued by the financial community, has also repeatedly spoken about it. He also expressed sympathy for the petition of the silver industry (Note 1). On the 11th of this month, a Reuters dispatch from New York reported that "The US Treasury Department needs 730,000,000 ounces of silver to complete its silver purchasing plan. A portion of it should be purchased from China. Although China is very willing to sell its silver reserve to the United States, it will inevitably have considerable exchange conditions." The above is the news about the new currency system for the past month.

On the 18th of this month, the Ministry of Finance officially announced a declaration, divided into three points:

(1) In order to fully maintain the credit of legal tender, the government's cash reserve shall be composed of gold, silver, and foreign exchange. The silver reserve should account for at least 25% of the total issuance.

(2) In order to facilitate merchants and the public, the government will mint half-yuan and one-yuan silver coins to complete the categories of hard currency.

(3) In order to enhance the consolidation of the legal tender's position, the government's cash reserve has already raised huge amounts of money, which will fully increase gold and foreign exchange.

In addition, there is one point that is very noteworthy, that is, the silver industry has repeatedly requested to revise the silver product management rules for several months, and it has been approved. In the future, the use of silver for silver products will still be handled according to the original practice.

According to a Washington National Electric telegram on the 18th, "Finance Minister H.H. Kung and representatives of the Chinese Ministry of Finance have established a Sino-US currency agreement. The content of which has long been eagerly awaited by the outside world, today has been released by Finance Minister H.H. Kung, saying that China and the United States have established an agreement, and the United States will begin to purchase a large amount of Chinese silver. The purpose of the purchase is to assist the Chinese government's new currency policy and to fulfill the Silver Purchase Act passed by the US Congress in 1934. The agreement is sufficient to assist the success of international currency stability, and later prepare to take the same action to stabilize currency with other countries, but separate talks with various countries are more appropriate than the method of international conferences, it is said. Mr. Kung then announced the amount of money to purchase Chinese silver, saying that he was prepared to pay in cash or US dollars, as for the quantity to be purchased, it will be kept secret! But it will be carried out immediately, and the price will be based on the monthly average price of the world market."

Summarizing the new developments of this currency system, there are the following three points:

(1) With the establishment of a currency agreement with the United States, the problem of the way out for China's silver reserve has been resolved. (Whether there are other conditions in the currency agreement is still unknown.)

(2) Restore the use of silver, one is to recast silver coins, and the other is that silver products are still handled according to the original practice.

(3) Clearly stipulate that the silver reserve accounts for 25% of the total issuance.

Now, let's examine these three points one by one.

First, the content of the Sino-US currency agreement is still unknown. The telegram only said that China's silver reserve can be sold to the United States. But the connection between the Sino-US currency values is a matter of course. Some say that the US currency has not yet reached a stable point, and the US President still has the possible power to devalue the US dollar by another 10%. In the event that the United States does devalue the currency, our exchange rate with other countries will also change accordingly. This is indeed possible. But when weighing two evils, choose the lesser, and when weighing two benefits, choose the greater. The most pressing issue for China's currency system is how to maintain foreign exchange reserves. Maintaining foreign exchange reserves still depends on the sale of silver reserves. If the silver price falls, it will be very unfavorable to us. And the foreign silver market has been manipulated by the United States, so there is no other way but to discuss with it. Otherwise, the future of the silver reserve is unknown. Whether the US dollar will be devalued again is a matter for the future, but the decision on the way out for the silver reserve is imminent. Weighing the pros and cons, this move cannot be said to be a misstep.

Second, the US silver purchasing policy was originally promoted by silver faction congressmen, and its origin should be political. Later, it combined the political purpose with the attempt of an international dual reserve system, the so-called expansion of the dollar group. The United States is very unfavorable to it. China was originally the largest silver-using country. If even silver products are prohibited, the United States will not be happy to hear it. With the establishment of this Sino-US currency agreement, our country announced the restoration of silver use, which may be one of the agreement conditions. As for minting silver dollars to represent the currency in circulation, although it does not harm the new currency system, it has only been half a year since the silver standard was abandoned. Now there is a sudden announcement of minting light-quality silver dollars, and the old silver dollars have not yet been completely collected. People in the interior, who are not enlightened, will inevitably be confused by this. The Ministry of Finance urgently needs to instruct local governments to clearly inform them so that people have something to follow.

Third, since the establishment of the new currency system, although the government has stated that the legal tender reserve is still 60% cash silver and 40% securities, the value of the silver reserve has actually been calculated according to the foreign exchange rate, and foreign exchange and gold have also been added to the reserve (the actual reserve required is only foreign exchange). Now it is clearly stipulated that the cash silver reserve should account for 25% of the total issuance. Originally, China had the possibility of fully adopting a foreign exchange reserve. Now, it has become a definite and undoubtedly dual reserve system. This is the most noteworthy point in the history of the new currency system. Since the US announced the silver purchasing policy, it immediately remembered the dual reserve system of four parts gold and one part silver. Its ambition is to promote it to various countries. The telegram said: "Later prepare to take the same action to stabilize currency with other countries, but separate talks with various countries are more appropriate than the method of international conferences." The establishment of this Sino-US currency agreement is a very good experience for the United States. Therefore, the Reuters telegram from the Shanghai Evening Post on the 21st reported that Biderman, the leader of the silver faction, declared: "This agreement is an example that Latin American countries should follow, and the case proposed by the United States at the London Economic Conference that the cash reserves of the central banks of various countries should maintain 20% silver is the basis of this agreement." According to a Washington National Electric telegram from the Great American Evening Post on the 19th, "Today the United States decided to begin the second step of the world currency stability work plan in order to restore international trade and seek world peace. The work plan was decided after signing the agreement to purchase silver with China. People here firmly believe that the United States will soon begin separate talks with the great powers on the issue of war debts owed by various countries to the United States in order to solve this difficult problem. Government officials today feel the same way that currency stability and the current state of international trade are deeply related to the solution of the war debt issue." The United States attempts to lead international currency: holding its two weapons—war debts and silver policy, and dealing with countries in the East and West. Now the silver policy has been successful, and it wants to further negotiate with various countries separately on the war debt issue in order to carry out its international dual-standard system. However, the suspicions of various countries are still deep, and the nationalistic fervor is still high. Various restrictions on international trade, such as tariff barriers, quota allocation systems, blocked accounts, and exchange restrictions, still exist. If only seeking the stability of international currency, whether it can be as the United States wishes is highly questionable. On the other hand, the dual-standard system has long been rejected by various countries. For the stability of international currency, European countries advocate the establishment of an international clearing bank through international common agreements, saving the use of cash, and still using the gold value standard. This is the opinion of general economists. It may not be able to coordinate with the US's proposal, and the US's attempt is obviously self-serving, and the political effect of the silver faction is also very profound. Whether European countries are willing to accommodate the US's proposal is also questionable. Although the United States can use war debts as a threat, various countries can delay and deny it, and there is nothing they can do. However, on the reverse side, in order to seek the stability of international currency, it is indispensable for those with gold strength like the United States to take the lead. Otherwise, the international deadlock will never be opened. However, leaders must have a spirit of sacrifice. If prejudices are too deep and they only seek profit, and want to use force to control various countries, and force them to follow me, it will eventually be in vain.

In terms of the dual-standard system, international common adoption is theoretically recognized by economists in various countries. The problem is whether the countries originally using gold have this need. They think that as long as the United States releases the gold in the vault, the international currency problem can be solved (this problem is very complicated and cannot be discussed in detail here). There is no need to adopt an international dual-standard system. Therefore, whether these two opinions can approach each other is still unknown. China's situation is different from that of gold-using countries. China originally used silver, and most of the reserve was originally cash silver. What is needed is how to obtain the supply of foreign exchange reserves. This time, the signing of a currency agreement with the United States is exactly what we need; for them, it is a touchstone for carrying out their international dual-standard system. The establishment of the agreement is not accidental. However, the United States believes that the success of the Sino-US currency agreement can be used as a precedent for separate negotiations with other countries; I am afraid it is too optimistic. As for us, we certainly hope it will succeed. (Yao Qingsan's "The Future of the New Monetary Policy in the Midst of Falling Silver Prices and the Proposal of a Dual Reserve System" in the Second Issue of the Third Volume of the Social Economic Monthly can be used as a reference.)

Finally, the United Kingdom did not express any opinion in advance on the establishment of this Sino-US currency agreement, and afterwards it praised it quite a bit. The establishment of China's new currency system has been mostly assisted by the United Kingdom. Now that China has signed a currency agreement with the United States, how can the United Kingdom be willing to do so? This point should be explored by the general public. In my opinion, the United Kingdom does not need to compete with the United States for China's currency system, nor can it compete with the United States. The pound and the US dollar have now stabilized at pre-war parity. If the monetary policies of both sides stabilize the currency with the US dollar, there is gradually no reason why it should not be stable with the pound. The United Kingdom sits back and enjoys the success, so why not sympathize with the United States? This is why the United Kingdom does not need to compete with the United States. The United States has the power to manipulate the world silver price, and the way out for China's silver reserve must be helped by the United States. The United Kingdom really cannot do anything. Last time, when the United States stopped purchasing silver in London, the London banking community wanted to unite and purchase it, but it was only a flash in the pan and there was no result. This is why the United Kingdom cannot compete with the United States. As for whether the United Kingdom and the United States had prior understanding, it is not known.

(Note 1) See the Financial Miscellany in the Fourth and Fifth Issues of the Third Volume of the Social Economic Monthly

On Minting Silver Coins 184

— Yu Qiong

The Ministry of Finance recently issued a declaration, stating the government's original intention to maintain the stability of currency value and to determine its independent autonomy, which shows that the government's determination to seek domestic economic stability is always based on consolidating the credit of the legal tender itself, and will never vacillate between countries or be an appendage of others. This policy of "self-reliance" should be learned by the people of the country. As for the three points declared, the first and third are both seeking to enrich the reserve and determine the basis of credit. This has always been the government's consistent policy and is the fundamental way to consolidate the credit of legal tender, so there is nothing to discuss. The second point is the reminting of new silver coins, which is not what the general public expected, and it is necessary to pay attention to it now. The original text said: "In order to facilitate merchants and the public, the government will mint half-yuan and one-yuan silver coins to complete the types of hard currency." When concentrating silver and strictly prohibiting the circulation of hard currency, suddenly declaring the reminting of silver coins will inevitably cause misunderstandings in many ways. Judging from the current domestic situation, it seems unnecessary to increase the minting of silver coins. Since the prohibition of silver coin circulation on November 4 last year, the circulation of the main and auxiliary legal tender has been unimpeded. Even in the stubborn poor materials that were usually considered to be accustomed to using hard currency, the promotion has been smooth and without difficulty, which proves that people can adapt to the new environment at any time. Since transactions have not been hindered, there is no need to mint silver coins to seek transaction convenience. Therefore, we infer that the intention in the middle may not be without international difficulties. However, it is useless to say what has been done. What we should pay attention to is the future problems and the location of the problems, and guide them according to the situation, so that we can remove the disadvantages and move to the benefits at any time. I humbly present several points as follows.

First, since the government implements coinage, it will inevitably issue circulation; otherwise, the cost of coinage will become a useless waste. Since what the Ministry of Finance has decided to mint is one-yuan and half-yuan silver coins, it can be known that they cannot be regarded as auxiliary coins. The government must stipulate the legal price of these silver coins in legal tender for circulation, and the two legal prices. How to always maintain their uniform circulation is a question worth considering. In our opinion, the new silver coins minted by the government must also be a named representative coin, whose actual value must be below the face value, but it still has a considerable amount of actual value. In the general psychology of the people, there may be biases. This is especially possible in general inland areas. Therefore, how to keep the prices of the two consistent at all times seems to be a question that should be considered. In our opinion, since the government has already reminted silver coins, the amount of silver coins and legal tender should each have considerable restrictions, so that the price of both will not be high due to the small quantity, and the price will not be cheap due to the large quantity. Before the new coins are minted in considerable quantities, it is not necessary to issue them for circulation for the time being, so as to prevent speculation and hoarding.

Second, the government is currently concentrating silver. At present, the purchasing power of legal tender and silver coins in the market is completely equal. Because there is no room for comparison in people's minds, they only know that paper money and silver coins represent the same meaning in transactions. Therefore, the concentration process is less difficult. If the newly minted silver coins representing the currency are issued for circulation in the market at this time, the new silver coins and the old silver coins will inevitably have an impression of currency depreciation, and they will change their past psychology and hoard the old silver coins tightly, which is tantamount to adding another layer of resistance to the concentration of cash. This is probably unavoidable by the facts. Therefore, we advocate that although the government has started minting silver coins, it does not have to rush to issue them for circulation, but in a short period of time, intensify the concentration of old silver coins, so as to avoid market confusion and self-destruction of the policy of concentrating cash. If silver coins of unequal value are forced to have equal market prices, then the old poor will hoard them tightly, which is unavoidable. The government's policy of concentrating cash will probably be destroyed by itself.

Third, at present, the external exchange rate of legal tender is maintained stable, which is a policy that we should always maintain. Legal tender cannot be cashed, but foreign exchange can be purchased at legal prices, which is the so-called foreign exchange standard. Although the newly minted representative silver coins can also purchase foreign exchange at the same legal price, they have a considerable amount of actual value, and the habit of using cash among the people has not been completely changed. I am afraid that after the new silver coins are issued, there will be a natural tendency to gradually flow into the inland rural areas, while legal tender will be mostly concentrated in cities that can be directly exchanged for foreign exchange at any time. If so, the rural currency and the urban currency will gradually differentiate in an invisible way, silver coins will circulate in the rural areas, and legal tender will circulate in the cities. I am afraid that over time, the circulation of legal tender in the inland will be harmed by silver coins. According to the actual environment of our country, this is very likely. How to prevent this natural differentiation of circulation areas is a question worth considering now.

Fourth, at present, the international situation is uncertain, and our country's position is particularly vulnerable to the influence of the international environment. According to the experience of various countries, when international relations change, the circulation of hard currency is most easily affected. For example, the US silver auxiliary coins in the Civil War era, although the difference between their face value and actual value was very large, they were all hidden in an instant. Another example is France during the European War. At first, in order to regulate the market, the central bank issued a large amount of silver coins, and the difference between the face value and the actual value was also large, but soon they were all hidden in secret and disappeared from the market. The new silver coins in our country, even if their face value is not based on their actual value, I am afraid that after international incidents occur, they will also be hidden and disappear, which will be enough to make the market rigid at first, transactions stagnant, and after a long time, there will inevitably be black market transactions, disrupting the market and hindering the circulation of legal tender. This is as clear as pointing to the palm, which can be foreseen. How to prevent this phenomenon from happening seems to be something to be considered repeatedly at this time.

Fifth, what is the fineness and weight of the new silver coins is currently unknown, but in fact, I am afraid that it will not be too low; if it is too low, it will inevitably have an impact on the psychology of the people. In the case that the cash - old silver coins have not been completely concentrated, if the price of the new silver coins is too low, it is enough to affect the people's confidence in the new currency system, because there is still a part of the old silver coins that can be compared in secret. If the price of the new silver coins is actually not very low, then the external value of the legal tender has obviously been restricted by this, and the flexibility of retreat. Then it is an undeniable fact. This point must also be considered at the beginning of coinage.

The above five points are our opinions on minting new silver coins. Judging from the facts, we deeply believe that it is unnecessary to mint silver coins. Since the implementation of the legal tender policy, the foreign exchange has been stable and the legal tender has been circulating unimpeded, sweeping away the mist of the silver standard for several years. In the future, as long as the exchange rate can be maintained stable externally and the financial institutions can be gradually improved internally to suit this brand-new system, the domestic economy can wait for the time to come. Minting silver coins seems to be unnecessary at present. However, we can adapt to changes and avoid the generation of future adverse effects at any time. There is still something to say, since the government announced the reminting of silver coins, the general discussion has misunderstood that this is related to the recent fall in silver prices. Some even said that the government could not sell silver, so it turned to minting silver coins, which is even more absurd. The value of our country's currency is purely unaffected by the price of silver. The high or low price of silver has absolutely no relationship with the value of our country's currency. Judging from our country at present, the rise and fall of silver prices are the same as the rise and fall of silk prices or tung oil prices. The high price of silver can indeed allow our country to gain more profits when selling silver, and we will inevitably suffer losses when the price of silver is low, but it is only limited to the less price obtained when selling silver coins, and it has absolutely no relationship with the currency system. Moreover, judging from the silver that can be sold at present, even if the silver price falls by half, the loss suffered by our country is probably not as large as the loss caused by the reduction of soybean exports from our country's international trade after the loss of the Northeast. Why should we be so worried about this? The reason for reminting silver coins is definitely not here. We can only recognize it as a kind of expedient policy of the government to cope with the international environment.

Securities: Spot Goods Dumped, Public Bonds Spiral Downward 185

Last week, from June 1st to 6th, the market situation of the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange fluctuated greatly. The situation in North China changed abruptly, and rumors in South China followed. These were embellished and filled with suspicion and fear. The Hong Kong market experienced massive changes, foreign exchange was in demand, and the public bond market experienced a significant drop. Although the bullish side is still struggling to move forward, it remains to be seen whether they can overcome this rough and dangerous path. According to observations of the current situation, most of the major players selling off in recent days are those with physical goods. For example, categories E and B of No. 47, categories C and D of No. 48, category A of the North Gang, and category D of No. 72 are substantial in number. According to the reporter's investigation, all of them need to recover cash. The retail investors are quite active, buying high and selling low, and fluctuating uncertainly. However, the bearish side with physical goods is unwilling to cover their positions unless at a considerable low price. Therefore, the future of the bond market is not optimistic due to the multiple uncertainties of the environment. Although the decline last week was relatively severe, it was still spiraling downward. On Monday, it fell by twelve to eight cents. On Tuesday, retail investors covered their short positions and the bullish side pushed up the price, increasing by as much as twenty-three to seven cents. The increase was too rapid, so it attracted large-scale selling from major players on Wednesday. All the gains of the previous day were lost. On Friday, rumors were rampant, and those with real strength sold off, mostly for this month, especially category E, which plummeted by sixty to seventy cents. On Saturday, the rumors did not subside, and the selling side was still strong, falling by about another half a dollar. As a result of the week's market prices, the overall decline ranged from forty-five cents to one dollar and forty cents. Category C for this month fell the most, by one dollar and forty cents, while category B for this month fell the least, by only forty-five cents. The total transaction volume was 39,415,000 yuan. Metals: Hunan Antimony Exports Are Quite Desolate 189

Hunan antimony is one of China's export metal products. In recent years, various countries have been relentlessly preparing for war, so the sales of this commodity to various countries in the East and West have been considerable. However, since the discovery of antimony mines in the Soviet Union and the Philippines, Hunan antimony has been hit hard, and sales have decreased. Overseas sales have been quite sluggish in recent weeks. According to various investigations, this is actually due to the fact that too much cargo was previously shipped, and it has not yet been completely sold. Fortunately, the sentiment in this port is good, and the inventory is also weak, so the selling price has not changed much. The current market price is 750 yuan per ton. Apart from sporadic transactions, there are very few large-scale transactions in the market.
